Overview of Economic Decline in Jiangxi Province: Food Imports Exceed 4 Million Yuan; Total Trade Volume Halved in Seven Years

Nanchang Communication: Jiangxi Province is an important agricultural region in the Yangtze River basin. Its economic structure is based on agricultural products, mainly rice. During its peak period, annual exports often reached 5 to 6 million yuan. Although it suffered from banditry in 1928, it still reached 1,670,1985 yuan. However, by 1933, it had decreased to over 3 million yuan, and in 1934, it was only over 800,000 yuan. The export figures of other agricultural by-products such as tobacco leaves, peanuts, vegetable oil, eggs, and bamboo and wood have also declined. Most farmers have become hungry vagrants, and imports exceed 4,030,000 yuan, mostly flour and foreign rice. It is strange for an agricultural province to have this phenomenon. Secondly, in terms of Jiangxi's specialty products, in 1928, the export volume of porcelain was 110,484 pieces, ramie cloth was 110,100 pieces, tea was 167,677 dan, and paper was 121,195 dan. However, in 1934, porcelain was only 35,271 pieces, ramie cloth was 5,246 pieces, tea was 87,646 dan, and paper was 49,368 dan. Furthermore, Jiangxi used to have the largest trade surplus due to its abundant agricultural products, prosperous handicrafts, and the frugality of its people. For example, in 1917, it was 14,966,563 yuan, in 1928 it was 15,120,669 yuan, and the surplus was often over one million yuan in other years. After 1931, it turned into a fixed trade deficit. In 1931, it was 215,239,111 yuan, and in 1932 it was 20,510,433 yuan. These figures indicate that Jiangxi has an outflow of 40 million yuan every year. If this continues, it will eventually be drained dry. Furthermore, the total trade volume of Jiangxi Province in 1928 was over 17,768,000 yuan, but last year it was only over 57,708,000 yuan, less than half. From this, it can be seen that the economic circulation power of Jiangxi Province has decreased by half, which is truly alarming.

Western Henan Highway to be Completed by Deadline; South Lin Highway to be Rerouted Through Yexian

Kaifeng Communication: In recent years, Henan Province has been actively building highways. National and provincial roads have been progressing rapidly. Road lines in eastern, southern, and northern Henan have long been open to automobile traffic. In the western Henan area, the Luoyang to Luoning section has been completed. However, the Changshui to Lushi and 閿鄉 to Lushi sections have been progressing slowly due to rugged mountain roads and difficult bridge and culvert construction. Since the establishment of the Northwest Bandit Suppression Headquarters, Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek has telegraphed the provincial government to complete all of the Western Henan Highway by December 15 of this year, as the transportation in the border area between Henan and Shaanxi is of great military importance. However, due to the remote location in the mountains and the difficulty in transporting bridge and culvert materials, Director Zhang Jingyu of the Department of Construction went to Luoyang on the 9th and inspected and urged along the 潼洛 Highway with District Commissioner 歐陽珍 of the Eleventh District, in order to complete the project as soon as possible. The Nanyang Highway runs east through Biyang to Zhumadian, south through Xinye to可達樊, and northeast through Fangcheng, Yexian, and Xuchang, directly to Kaifeng. However, the northwest is mountainous and transportation is inconvenient. The original South Lin Highway, namely Nanyang to Linru, via Nanzhao, Lushan, and Baofeng, was estimated to require 1,520,000 yuan for stone culverts and bridges. It has now been decided to reroute it northwest from Yexian to Linru. In addition to the existing road line between Nanyang and Yexian, 800,000 yuan is enough for the section between Yexian and Linru. It is heard that the plan has been roughly finalized and will be implemented soon. (October 12)

Suspicion of Mailing Morphine Leads to Arrest

Songjiang: Abbot 恆光 of the Ci Yuan Temple at 爱民 Bridge in Songjiang, a native of Sichuan, was recently arrested by the Public Security Bureau under secret orders. A letter from Sichuan was found in the temple. The authorities initially kept the case secret. It is now known that the monk received a letter from a Mr. Liu in Sichuan, stating that he had over one hundred taels of white fungus and would send it to Songjiang in a few days. After receiving it, he was asked to notify a Mr. Wang in Shanghai, who would send someone to Songjiang to pick it up in person. Unexpectedly, the white fungus sent by Mr. Liu was actually morphine. The post office discovered it en route and reported it to the county government for investigation. Today (14th), Investigator Zhang of the county government interrogated the monk, who denied it from beginning to end, and was ordered to be returned to custody for further investigation.

Resolution of National Goods Dispute

Wuxi: The dispute between the Shanghai National Goods Promotion Association and local silk, cloth, department store, and other industries has been resolved through the best efforts of party, government, and commercial sectors, and it was decided to conclude it on the 16th. County Magistrate Wang was responsible for persuading, but the association suddenly denied the Chamber of Commerce's mediation, causing the dispute to arise again. Yesterday, the Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the county government, requesting that the case be investigated and dealt with in accordance with the precedents of Zhenjiang, Huaiyin, and Nantong, and that the association's itinerant vendors who were disguised as auctioneers in Wuxi be expelled to ensure commercial stability. Otherwise, the standing members of the association would have to submit their resignations at the members' meeting on the 15th to allow the various industries to decide for themselves. At the same time, telegrams were sent to the chambers of commerce in Changzhou, Yixing, Jiangyin, Liyang, Zhenjiang, and Nantong counties, urging them to lead the various industries to unite and act in unison, and to request the ministry and province to strictly ban such activities to avoid disruption. On one side, Cheng Jingtang and Xue Mingjian were sent to Shanghai to urge Qian Chengxu, the chairman of the association, to come to Wuxi for further mediation. By 4:00 PM, Qian and others had arrived in Wuxi. After mediation at the County Chamber of Commerce, the association followed the instructions of the party and government mediation and closed its business on the 15th and ended on the 16th. Thus, a national goods auction dispute was completely resolved.

Details of Group of Swindlers on Inland River Steamers

Suzhou: Recently, there have been groups of swindlers posing as sick people and selling fake medicine on inland river steamers such as Suzhou-Wuxi and Suzhou-Changshu. These people make a profit of about one hundred yuan every day. At the same time, the number of victims is unknown. A woman from the Dongjiang 涇乡 village in the Su-Chang border area recently lost her relative so she borrowed 33 silver dollars from relatives to come to Suzhou. They met these people on the steamer, only bought a so-called Tibetan incense for one yuan, but the remaining 32 yuan were stolen by opportunity. They reported to the Changshu Public Security Bureau, which sent a letter to the detective team here. On the night of the 13th, the captain and detectives of the Wu County Detective Team arrested seven people, including 弃永明, at the 大新 Hotel outside the 城門, and seized more than two hundred packages of fake Tibetan incense. After taking the team, they were sent to the Wu County Public Security Bureau on the 14th for interrogation.

Details of Bandit Robbery on Highway Automobile

Pinghu: At 3:28 PM on the National Day, the Jia-Hu intermodal transport vehicle from Zhapu Station to Shanghai was robbed by bandits in the 涇地方 area. The reports in the Shanghai-Hangzhou newspapers vary. It has now been confirmed that the vehicle was No. 61305. When driving to the 57-kilometer mark of Jinshanwei, a bandit wearing a long robe suddenly pulled out a pistol and forced the car to stop. At the same time, three other bandits wearing felt hats also pulled out guns. After the car stopped, another bandit boarded the car, pulled out a large machete from his clothes, broke the tire, and began to search the passengers for more than 2,300 silver dollars. When they left, they fired four shots as a warning. The passengers' luggage was taken away. Helpless, they changed to a return vehicle to Zha. When they got off the bus at the station, everyone was terrified.

Public Concession Will Soon Conduct Census; Age and Category Must Be Filled in; Authorities Attach Importance to Co-Residence Situation

The household registration survey of residents in the Public Concession is held every five years as usual. This year is the year to hold the survey. It has now been scheduled to be held on the 23rd of this month. The household registration survey forms will be distributed to each household in the Concession on the morning of the 22nd of this month, and the investigators will collect them from each household on the morning of the 24th. The household registration survey form is printed in four languages: Chinese, English, Japanese, and Russian. However, this year's survey scope is slightly wider than the previous one in 1930. In the first half of this year, the Board of Directors of the Municipal Council decided that in this year's household registration survey form, both Chinese and foreign residents should fill in the age category, and it plans to invite the Shanghai Municipal Government and the French Concession authorities to cooperate and provide coordinated statistical materials, in order to improve the completeness of this year's survey results, and to focus especially on the age category and the population density of each district. The authorities in China and France have now agreed to cooperate. The main points of the new changes in this year's household registration survey form are briefly explained as follows: (1) In the Chinese form, the previous two categories of children and adults have been cancelled and replaced by age categories, which are divided into four items: under five years old, five to fifteen years old, fifteen to twenty years old, and over twenty years old. (2) In the Chinese form, previously, servants were listed separately from other residents in the house. This distinction no longer exists because it is not related to the calculation of each person. The total number of servants can be seen in the occupation item. (3) The Municipal Council attaches great importance to several families living in one house. Therefore, a column for the number of co-residing households has been added to the previous servant item. In addition, there are also types of occupations, etc., which, along with the age category and the number of attached households, etc., are not available in the previous survey form. Furthermore, the English survey form opens with the age category, which is divided into five items. When filling it out, just tick a "×" in the box that your age belongs to, without having to fill in the exact age. The Westerner each wishes to show their actual age. When investigating the population last time, many obstacles occurred, that is why, All the distribution and collection of survey forms are managed by the Police Department of the Municipal Council. In addition, the calculation of foreign people on roads outside the concession is obtained by the method of communication. The number of troops stationed in various countries is also obtained from the commanders of the troops stationed in various countries.

Japanese Restrict Chinese People from Going to Dalian; Crack Down on Entry of Laborers, etc.

Shanghai to Dalian ships, such as the British Taikoo Company and the Japanese Dalian Steamship Company and Nisshin Steamship Company, used to sell tickets to passengers for boarding, regardless of first, second, or third class and steerage. There were no restrictions. Only when it was considered that there was an epidemic would the passengers be tested for feces. There were no other regulations prohibiting entry. The incident of Yingkou prohibiting a large number of Zhilu farmers from entering the country gradually spread to Dalian and Shanghai. The Dalian authorities have also implemented harsh restrictions on Chinese passengers traveling to Dalian by ship from Shanghai, ordering various shipping companies not to sell Dalian tickets indiscriminately. It is investigated that those who are restricted are designated as Chinese laborers, farmers, and small vendors who travel in third-class cabins and steerage who want to go to Guanwai to make a living are not allowed to take ships to Dalian, while passengers in first and second class cabins are not restricted by this ban. Last month, British and Japanese ships carried passengers to Dalian, and the Chinese passengers in steerage were not allowed to enter the country and were returned to Shanghai. Many people have been detained for lack of travel expenses and acquaintances. Therefore, various shipping companies have now strictly cracked down on all Chinese who purchase third-class tickets or steerage tickets, and they must state that they have a job in Dalian before they are allowed to board the ship, otherwise they will be refused to sell tickets.

Preventing Abuses of False Claims of Poverty: Paupers Cannot be Exempted from Guarantees to Receive Permits; Vagrants are Sent Directly to Hospitals for Treatment; Public Safety Bureau Submits Report to the Municipal Government Based on Discussions

According to the Xin Sheng News Agency, the Special Trades Association of this city stated that due to the large number of poor people in this city and the strict enforcement of opium suppression, most poor people need guarantors to issue certificates when applying for opium suppression permits and filling out certificates. It is difficult to register because of the difficulty in finding a guarantor. If the guarantee for poor people to receive permits is cancelled, the registrants will be very enthusiastic, which is very convenient for the future of opium suppression. The Special Trades Association submitted a document stating the reasons, requesting the municipal government to approve the cancellation of the guarantee for poor people to receive permits. The municipal government specially ordered the Public Safety Bureau to review and reply. According to the provisions of Article 5, Paragraph 2 of the time limit for registering opium users, which states that a certificate must be filled out by the head of the Jia (25 households) and the head of the Bao (100 households) to be eligible for the permit. However, this city has not yet implemented the Baojia system, so poor people are allowed to receive permits. As long as the poor people’s relatives and friends have occupations and addresses, they can be guarantors. Therefore, when the poor people receive the permits, they only need the guarantor to prove and fill out the certificate, and they can be allowed to issue the permit. Since its implementation, the number of registrants has been dominated by poor people and there is no obstruction. Because no matter how poor a person is, it is unlikely that there is no one they know in the whole city. If they are vagrants and beggars, they have no fixed residence and no fixed occupation, so it is difficult to find a guarantor. Therefore, the Public Safety Bureau specifically exempts these poor people from guarantee and sends them directly to the opium suppression hospital for treatment. According to the original regulations, restricting the poor to receive permits requires a guarantee to prevent opium users from buying and claiming to be poor to receive permits. If no one proves, then all opium users can claim to be poor to receive permits, which will cause great abuses and unimaginable consequences. Therefore, the request of the Special Trades Association to cancel the guarantee is difficult to handle. The Public Safety Bureau has now submitted the detailed situation to the Municipal Government.

Salt Affairs Audit Office: Completion of Salt Mounds Construction in Huaibei; Construction of Jiangnan Along the River Has Now Started; Sailboat Workers’ Unemployment is Being Planned for Relief

According to the Da Gong News Agency, in order to increase salt production in the salt areas, the General Office of Salt Affairs Audit of the Ministry of Finance is building salt mounds on both banks of the Huaibei and Jiangnan along the river. The north bank has been completed, and the construction of the south bank has begun. After the transportation was changed to wheel transportation, more than 10,000 sailboat workers were unemployed. The Ministry of Finance plans to provide relief. Yesterday, Director of the Audit Office Zhu Tingqi gave a detailed account of the process to the reporter of the Da Gong News Agency, which is recorded as follows:

Huaibei Completed, Jiangnan Started. The two Huai Rivers and other places bordering Jiangsu and Anhui provinces in my country are famous salt producing areas. The annual output value reaches several million, but the loss of production is very large due to poor refining. Therefore, in order to increase national income, the Salt Affairs Audit Office of the Ministry of Finance is building several salt mounds on both banks of the Huai River to produce and manufacture salt at any time. The north bank has been completed and the construction of the south bank has begun, which is expected to be completed this year.

Sailboat Workers’ Unemployment, Seeking Relief. Regarding the transportation and sale of salt produced in the salt area to the market, the use of sailboats will delay the voyage time, which will affect the economic time of the salt workers. Therefore, it is changed to wheel transportation. As a result, tens of thousands of sailboat workers who depend on this over-production are suddenly unemployed. The Salt Office once advocated building a hemp bag factory to try to accommodate them. However, the number of people is too large and they are new to the work, making it difficult to realize. The sailboat workers have repeatedly petitioned the central government for relief, but a concrete solution has not yet been reached. The Ministry of Finance is now deliberating on a proper relief plan so that the sailboat workers can have a way out in life.

Wen Zhao Road People's Education Center: Promotes Public Labor Service; Organizes Public Education Team and Lecture Team; Starts Working Simultaneously on the First Day of Next Month

According to the Shen Shi News Agency, the Municipal People's Education Center, in order to use the spare time of citizens, promote the spirit of labor service, instill modern knowledge in the general public, and cultivate healthy citizens, plans to organize a public education team and a public lecture team from the first day of next month to teach and lecture to various households in the city in order to achieve the purpose of public labor service. The details are recorded as follows:

Education Team. The main tasks of the team are divided into (1) literacy teaching, (2) common sense guidance, and (3) household assistance. It is planned to establish a large team, which will be divided into two medium teams, and each medium team will have ten small teams. Each small team will have three people, a total of 30 teams and 90 people. The standard for participating team members is children between the ages of 9 and 12, and it is planned to target various families in the city.

Lecture Team. The focus of the team's work is to use citizens to promote the spirit of labor service and instill new knowledge in general. Its organization is similar to that of the public education team. The large team is divided into three medium teams, and each medium team is divided into ten small teams, a total of 30 teams and 90 people. However, the standard for participating team members is junior high school graduates aged 20 to 40, and the Public Education Center will specify the lecture materials and assign the team members to lecture in designated areas. They must also fill out work reports every day.

Industry and Commerce: Practical Problems Research Class Starts; Organized by the Industrial and Commercial Revival Association

The Industrial and Commercial Revival Committee established by the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, in order to train basic commercial talents and study practical problems in industry and commerce, proposed a method for running the research class by the heads of the training group, Luo Qinghua and Pan Yangyao. After the small group committee passed it, it was decided to co-organize with the Chamber of Commerce Commercial School and invite experts to serve as lecturers. It is now scheduled to start registration from the 15th of this month. The method is as follows:

Brief Rules. Brief rules for the practical problems research class in industry and commerce: (1) Purpose: To study practical problems in industrial and commercial management, commodity marketing, and industrial and commercial accounting in order to increase the service capabilities of service personnel and promote the revival of industry and commerce. (2) Students: Managers of industrial and commercial institutions, and shop assistants, factory workers, and assistants. (3) Classes: According to current needs, temporarily divided into three classes: industrial and commercial management, commodity marketing, and industrial and commercial accounting. (4) Research class: Each class is set for ten weeks. (5) Research time: Each class is twice a week, set from 7:00 PM to 9:00 PM every day. (6) Enrollment: Each class will start with 30 students. (7) Certificate: Students who have completed the research period and passed the exam will be issued a certificate by the association. Those with excellent grades will be given awards by the association. (8) Fees: Each person should pay a research and lecture fee of 4 yuan per class. If they are willing to attend two classes, they will pay 6 yuan. If they are willing to attend all three classes, they will pay 8 yuan. However, those who are recommended by members of the Chamber of Commerce will receive a 50% discount. (9) Registration: From October 15 to October 24. Registration location: Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Commercial Night School. (10) Start date: October 28.

Lecturers. (1) Lecturers for the industrial and commercial management class: Cao Yunxiang, He Qingnuo, Cheng Shouchong, Tu Zheyin, Mo Ruoqiang, Cao Yimin, Qu Kegong, Tang Yichong, Kong Shi'e, Zhu Xianfang, Zhang Sumin. (2) Lecturers for the commodity marketing class: Gao Shiheng, Xu Xiaochu, Xu Baiyi, Wang Xingyao, Lu Qianli, Jin Runxiang, Chen Xiaodie, Li Kangnian, Zheng Chengqing, Ren Jinpin. (3) Lecturers for the industrial and commercial accounting class: Xie Lin, Pan Xulun, Xu Yongzuo, Xi Yushu, Li Wenjie, Li Hongshou, Jin Zongcheng, Lu Shanshi, Wang Enfang, Wu Sheng, Xu Shequn, Dong Xianmo. (4) Special lecturers for each class: Pan Gongzhan, Wang Yunwu, Zhang Naiqi, Dai Zhisai, Xu Peikun, Chen Diexian, Qing Linian, Yang Yinpu, Wang Yansong, Luo Qinghua, Pan Yangyao.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce: Instructions on Doubts about Stamp Tax Application

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to Zhenfeng Electrical Manufacturing Factory yesterday, instructing on five points of doubt about stamp tax application: On the 12th of this month, we received your letter inquiring about five points regarding stamp tax. Our reply is as follows: (1) Because of the difficulties for the consignee to affix the stamp tax on the goods receipt, it is proposed to change to a delivery book, with each book affixed with 2 jiao. This matter has already been reported to the Ministry of Finance by our association, but it has not been approved. (2) In commercial transactions that do not use cash, but are paid at the end of the month according to custom, and a detailed account of the product name, quantity, and price is issued to the customer before the deadline, this is the bill for payment mentioned in Article 16, Section 3 of the Stamp Tax Law and should be affixed with a stamp tax according to the regulations in the tax rate table. (3) The workers' work booklets issued to workers, if the workers use them to withdraw wages, do not need to be affixed with stamp tax according to the provisions in the tax exemption column of Article 16, Section 4 of the Stamp Tax Law. (4) The workers' workbooks used in factories cannot be exempted from stamp tax by analogy with the workers' work booklets for withdrawing money, and there has been a ministry approval. (5) According to the interpretation of the Ministry of Finance, documents are divided into internal use and external use, while account books are used for internal audit and there is no distinction between internal and external. Therefore, all account books related to business should be affixed with stamp tax and cannot be excused as internal use and exempted. According to the above reasons, the material inquiry account book should be affixed with stamp tax, etc.

Wusong Rent Reduction Dispute Resolved; Ren Changhe Property Reduced by 20% Across the Board

The city houses in the Baima Road East Section Ferry Terminal area of Wusong are owned by Ren Changhe Company. The monthly rent is more than 20 yuan. Recently, due to the sluggish market, the impact has spread to Wusong City and business has been unusually quiet. The tenants there, Xie Xing Shun Brick and Tile Shop, Mingyuan Tea House, Zhongxin Hotel, Changji Timber Shop, Jiang Gongxing Customs Broker, etc., jointly submitted a request to various party, government, and police agencies this spring, requesting Ren Changhe to reduce the rent. Because the landlord did not agree, it has been brewing for half a year. The Eighth District Party Department of Wusong, considering the decline in business in Wusong City and the need to resolve the rent reduction dispute, convened both parties yesterday at the District Party Department for a meeting. Representatives of the landlord, Zhao Weixuan, and the heads of the tenants and the District Party Department, Wang Chenge, etc., attended the meeting. The results of the meeting were: (1) All future rents will be reduced by 20% (Ren Changhe property). (2) The rent owed by the tenants will be paid off in two installments. (3) After the rent reduction, the tenants must not be in arrears again. After the decision, both parties expressed satisfaction and dispersed.

Summary of Activities of Various Charity Organizations

The Fundraising Division of the China Huayang Joint Famine Relief and Disaster Relief General Association has received enthusiastic support from all walks of life since the fundraising for the Jianghe flood disaster began. Mrs. Wang Zhengxu, Chairman of the Shanghai Women's Association, and members of the association have always been enthusiastic about public welfare. In view of the severe flood this year, they launched a fundraising campaign and raised 960 yuan in just a few days. Feeling that this was not enough, they held a tea dance party at the Paramount Hotel. The ticket sales revenue, after deducting necessary expenses, had a net surplus of 2,056 yuan, which, together with the donations, totaled 3,016 yuan. The full amount was submitted to the Fundraising Division for disaster relief. In addition, the Chinese Red Cross Society allocated 40,000 yuan for disaster relief to the General Association for distribution to Shandong, Hubei, Hunan, and Jiangsu provinces, each receiving one-fourth. They have been received and remitted to the branches of the General Association in Shandong, Hubei, and Hunan provinces for distribution. The disaster relief funds for Jiangsu province are directly remitted to the disaster area. It is reported that the Red Cross Society will continue to allocate flour, clothing, medicine, etc. to the General Association for distribution to the above-mentioned four provinces.

The Huayang Joint Famine Relief Association believes that although the Yangtze River has receded, disaster relief should be carried out actively. However, the disaster area is too large and the resources are limited. Except for Hubei, Hunan, Jiangxi and other provinces that have jointly handled the matter with the Red Swastika Society, Hubei, the gateway to disaster, has suffered the most severely. The association first sent a special commissioner to cooperate with the Jisheng Society. According to the report of the commissioner Zheng Shouchuan after his departure, which is excerpted as follows: He arrived in Wuhan on the 6th and transferred to a small steamer to reach Tianmen County, a winding waterway of 360 li. Along the way, there were many breaches on both banks, and the area behind the embankment was a vast expanse of water. Most of the victims were temporarily living in straw sheds or small boats. The various tragic situations are difficult to describe in detail. The county is divided into eight districts, and the most severely affected are the first, fifth, and eighth districts, followed by the second and fourth districts, and then the third, sixth, and seventh districts. This joint release is aimed at the first, fifth, and eighth districts. However, the first and eighth districts have been surveyed and released by Daoist Hou and his colleagues from the Jisheng Society, and most of them have been completed. Shouchuan has set off to survey the fifth district. The disaster area of the county is more than 6,300 square li, accounting for about nine-tenths of the county. It is estimated that about 1.5 million mu of farmland have been flooded. The loss of damaged houses, property, and livestock is no less than 245 million yuan. The total population of the county is more than 800,000, and more than 600,000 people have been affected. The number of people who drowned is estimated at 12,000. Although the water has receded, there are still one or two feet of water in the low-lying areas. Looking at the vastness of the disaster area and the cause of the disaster, it seems difficult to solve the problem with the amount of disaster relief. It is difficult to estimate the number of people without food, clothing, or homes. In the blink of an eye, autumn is over and winter is coming. The plight of hunger and cold is so tragic that it is unbearable to imagine.

The Chinese Jisheng Society believes that the flood in Tianmen, Hubei is severe, and the society has cooperated with Huayang Joint Famine Relief to remit 9,000 yuan for disaster relief and 2,000 yuan raised by Hou Yongde, the abbot of the Changchun Temple in Wuchang, totaling 12,000 yuan, all of which were used to purchase soybeans and rice for distribution, as reported in the previous newspaper. Recently, the association received a letter from Hou Yongde, the director of disaster relief in Tianmen, stating that the villagers in the Yuxin River area of the eighth district posted notices on the 30th, stating that the distribution would be held from October 1 to 5. The distribution locations were divided into two places, one at the Futaiyuan Rice Shop in Dongguan and the other at the District Office of the Eighth District. In total, 1,036 bean and rice disaster relief tickets were collected in five days, including 5,741 large tickets and 2,715 small tickets, with a total of 70 shi, 0 dou, 9 sheng, and 8.5 ge of rice and beans distributed. However, there was a lot of loss of beans and rice, and the actual distribution was 73 shi, 4 dou, and 9 ri of rice and 77 bai, 6 dou, and 9 sheng of broad beans. The fifth district (i.e., the Ganziyi area) dispatched Daoist Liu Xingben and others to investigate on the 6th. It was found that the Yuxin River area in the eighth district is relatively high, and the autumn crops planted can withstand drought and the seedlings are also lush. It is expected to mature around October 20. The buckwheat has also been moistened by the heavy rain on September 30, and a good harvest is expected next year. The people in the district have no worries about food. The first district is slightly lower and has suffered another flood, resulting in a loss of most of the autumn harvest. The fifth district has a history of low land and no harvest at all. Hanchuan is located to the east of Damenchen County and borders the fifth district. The terrain is even lower and is still a vast ocean. The disaster is no less severe than that of Tianmen. However, it is slightly further away from the breach, and people were able to relocate after the breach, resulting in fewer deaths. Most of the people in Tianmen City live by manual weaving, but at present, the Baiye industry is depressed and life is hopeless. The rice and beans distributed this time are just a drop in the bucket and cannot solve the problem. It is hoped that all the philanthropists will call for donations to provide a continuous supply of disaster relief food and drink.

The fundraising team of the flood disaster relief association received a letter from the Wei Er He Ji Textile Factory yesterday, which read: Dear Sir, in the face of the tragic flood this year, all colleagues should emulate cotton and linen. Guangdong Bank: Creditors Held a Talk Yesterday; Three Groups from the Kwong Siu Association Form a Debt Collection Group; Written Opinions Solicited for Further Discussion at a Meeting

According to the Xin Xin News Agency, since the Guangdong Bank ceased operations, creditors of the Shanghai branch have registered with the Kwong Siu Association, the Guangdong Fellow Villagers Association, the Yue Qiao Commercial Federation, and other three groups, requesting them to preside over everything. The three groups specially convened a talk with the creditors of the Guangdong Bank at the Kwong Siu Association on Ningbo Road at 4:00 PM yesterday. Wen Qinfu of the Kwong Siu Association, Jiang Tianduo of the Guangdong Fellow Villagers Association, Chen Bingqian of the Yue Qiao Commercial Federation, and more than 100 creditors including Tang Haian attended the meeting. Chen Bingqian, who was elected as chairman, reported briefly that since the Yue Qiao and other three groups have been handling the registration of creditors of the Guangdong Bank, as of the 13th of this month, a total of 732,456 yuan, 7 jiao, and 8 fen have been registered. As of the 14th, a total of 75,721 yuan and 8 jiao and 1 fen have been registered, totaling 800,08,178 yuan and 5 jiao and 9 fen. Among them, fixed deposits accounted for about 420,000 yuan, current deposits accounted for about 185,000 yuan, and transactions and drafts accounted for about 203,000 yuan. Today's talk with the creditors is to solicit opinions from the creditors in order to proceed. After the chairman's report, the creditors expressed many opinions, which were roughly divided into (1) supporting the resumption of business by the Guangdong Bank, with three-quarters or half of the deposits used as capital. The Guangdong Bank currently has assets of more than 22 million yuan and liabilities of more than 14 million yuan. According to the current value of the industry, only more than 8 million yuan can be used to offset the arrears, resulting in considerable losses. (2) Opposing the use of deposits as capital, hoping to implement liquidation and return the arrears. After the chairman summarized the opinions of everyone, a unanimous resolution was reached: (1) The Kwong Siu Association and other three groups are also one of the creditors and should form a debt collection group with the creditors to proceed together. (2) Send letters to each creditor soliciting written opinions on the two items of liquidation and resumption of business, and then hold a meeting to vote. The meeting ended at about 6:00 PM.

Notice from the Two-Route Administration: Measures for Accepting and Transporting Banknotes

The Two-Route Administration yesterday notified all sections and stations that passengers are still allowed to carry banknotes with them at their own discretion. However, if passengers voluntarily submit banknotes to the station for transportation, the station should accept them and collect freight according to regulations, charging one-tenth of the freight rate for currency. The Central Bank may still transport silver coins and banknotes free of charge. For the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the Farmers Bank of China, silver coins should still be charged at 60% of the standard rate, while banknotes should be charged at one-tenth of the currency rate, further discounted by 60%. However, the preferential treatment for the Farmers Bank of China should follow the provisions of the previous notice until the end of October of this year. All departments are instructed to comply with these instructions.

Fire on Zhangjiabang Road, Dongjiadu

At 9:50 AM yesterday, a fire broke out in the back of the firewood shop opened by Zhang Xisheng, a local resident, at No. 1011 Zhangjiabang Road, behind the Sanguantang in Dongjiadu, Pudong. The piled firewood caught fire and quickly spread out of control. The Pudong Fire Brigade was notified and dispatched Director Zhao and a team of firefighters with a pump truck to the scene. Fortunately, the location was close to Zhangjiabang, making it convenient to draw water. The firefighters were able to calmly extinguish the fire. The Yangjingzhen Fire Brigade also arrived with a truck to assist. After burning for about an hour, in addition to the complete destruction of the firewood shop, a dim sum shop next door to the north, an empty house, and two thatched houses in the back were also destroyed. The houses on both the north and south ends were saved. After the fire was extinguished, the Sanguantang police station took Zhang to the station for questioning. Zhang insisted that the fire started in the thatched house in the back. The police station dispatched police to summon the residents of the thatched house, but they could not be found. Zhang was then sent to the Tangqiao police station for further investigation.

Death of Dai Hainan: French Concession Police Sue Chauffeur

Dai Hainan, a 17-year-old student at Zhaohe Middle School residing at No. 17 Gengyuli, Rue Puteaux in the French Concession, was passing by the tram turn at the Bund outside the French Concession on the afternoon of the 5th of this month, at 6:00 PM. A tram No. 48 on Route 10 of the French Commercial Tram Company, driven by Xu Muqing, was turning east, traveling south. At the same time, a cargo truck No. 6038 (British Concession Permit) 1195 (French Concession Permit) driven by Peng Taoyuan from Tongzhou, (belonging to Peng Guiji, a transporter at No. 19 Maktout Road, Dixi'en Road, Hongkou) was also turning east in the same direction as the tram. The two vehicles collided and trapped him in the middle, causing him to be injured. He was sent to Guangci Hospital in a police vehicle, but died on the 7th due to ineffective treatment. His body was sent to the morgue. The police investigation found that the fault lay with the truck, and the driver, Peng Taoyuan, was sent to the Second Special District Court for interrogation. Yesterday afternoon, Judge of the Third Branch, attended the Criminal Court to try the case. Attorney Yuan Jiahan from the Police Department explained the case, and filed a public prosecution according to Article 276, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Code for causing death due to professional negligence. The victim's father, Shu Xinggeng (45 years old, a businessman in his hometown who came to Shanghai after receiving the news), also hired lawyer Sun Zuji to file a private prosecution. He calculated the loss based on the deceased's potential earnings of thirty yuan per month until the age of 60, assuming he would serve society until the age of 60, amounting to 35 years and a total of 12,600 yuan, plus funeral expenses of 386.5 yuan. He requested that the court order the defendant Peng Taoyuan and the owner of the truck, Peng Guiji, to pay the compensation. The defendant testified that the truck had already passed in front of the tram and that it was the tram's fault. However, witnesses Xu Yuexiao, the tram driver from the tram company, and Luo Zifan, the ticket seller, testified that the tram was in front and the truck was behind, and that the truck caused the accident. Furthermore, the victim shouted that he was hit by the truck after being struck. The court also summoned witnesses Li Xueyi, Han Zhongtao, Chen Zigen, and Chen Ayu, who were truck workers, and questioned them separately. Their testimonies were the same as the defendant's. The court decided to adjourn the hearing to the 18th for further inquiry. The defendant was remanded in custody.

Sun Bingxiang from Ningbo attempted to sell ten counterfeit banknotes of a certain bank, each worth one yuan, to his fellow villager Lu Xiaocai in Lane 59, Haining Road, for profit at around 7:00 PM on the 5th of this month. When questioned, the defendant insisted that he bought the counterfeit banknotes for three yuan and intended to resell them to Lu Xiaocai for a small profit, requesting leniency. Joint Production and Sales of Matches: Business Gradually Recovering; Foreign Merchants' Dumping Declining; Branch Offices Being Established in Tianjin and Other Places

Dagong News Agency reports that the domestic match factories, including Dachunghua, Zhengda, Zhongguo, Tongsui, Huai Shang, Dahua, Minsheng, and Daming, have been formally operating under a joint production and sales cooperative policy since the establishment of an office on July 11th of this year. Shanghai Public Security Bureau to Establish Police Museum: Displaying Various Weapons, Drugs, Counterfeit Currency, and Other Items

Guomin News Agency reports that Cai Jinjun, Director of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau, in order to clarify all the weapons used in theft and robbery and to ensure that the police have the necessary knowledge for identification and strict prevention, has established a police "museum" in the left-side stable of the bureau. The Municipal Government has approved the allocation of funds for this project. However, due to limited financial resources, it is not possible to fully equip the museum. Therefore, the bureau is temporarily collecting various weapons used by thieves and other illegal items from the confiscated evidence of the First Special District Court, the Second Special District Court, the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, the Municipal Security Department, and the Third Section of the bureau. These items will be numbered and displayed in glass display cases. The police commissioner is responsible for managing the museum. A report of the reporter’s visit to the museum yesterday is recorded below:

Thieves' Weapons: Various genuine and fake firearms, pliers, iron rulers, iron bars, iron hammers, sharp knives of various sizes, iron hooks, rope ladders, long and short iron drills, and other iron tools are too numerous to mention. All items are numbered and placed in glass display cases for identification.

Highly Toxic Drugs: There are also highly toxic drugs from confiscated evidence from various agencies, such as large and small red pills, heroin, morphine, and opium dross. There are also various models of equipment for manufacturing red pills, heroin, and morphine, such as iron sieves, in various shapes and colors.

Counterfeit Currency Models: As for the counterfeit currency display, there are counterfeit banknotes of ten yuan and five yuan denominations from various banks in China, such as the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the Bank of Central and South China. The colors are bright, and the manufacturing is exquisite, making it difficult to distinguish between genuine and fake. There are also many models of counterfeit banknotes from various banks, as well as substandard overseas Chinese silver coins and models of their manufacturing.

Detective Research: Of particular note are two glass panes, each with three bullet holes. These allow detectives to use scientific methods to study and determine the order of firing (first shot, second shot, third shot) on each pane of glass, as well as other studies of assumed criminal footprints. By measuring the size and length of the footprints, the height and build of the perpetrator can be estimated.

Crime Identification: A map is hung in the museum, showing the locations of various crimes committed within the municipality, marked with different symbols. This allows viewers to see at a glance which areas have the highest number of kidnapping cases, robbery cases, theft cases, and drug cases, allowing the relevant sub-bureaus or police stations to be instructed to strengthen their vigilance and take strict precautions.

Official Police Uniforms: There are also two models of the uniforms worn by the bureau's officials and police officers, dressed in full attire, with shoulder straps, leather shoes, hat styles, and waist belts, arranged in a rectangular glass case.

High Tide Yesterday Afternoon: Roads Continued to be Flooded; Tide Receded After 4 PM

Datong News Agency reports that the high tide in the Huangpu River yesterday morning and afternoon reached close to the shore, and the low-lying roads were flooded by water flowing back from the sewers. Yesterday, the tide rose twice. The early tide was at 1:15 AM, and the volume reached only 10 feet 7 inches, still far from the shore. No water flowed out of the ditches on the low-lying roads. At 1:36 PM, the afternoon tide suddenly rose to about 12 feet, exceeding the early tide by about a foot. The low-lying roads continued to be flooded by water flowing back from the sewers. The flooding was most severe on the side of Wing On Company on Nanjing Road. There was also water flowing out in front of the new customs gate on the Bund. The flooding began to recede after 4 PM.

Death in Bathhouse Over a Bar of Soap: Rubdown Turns Fatal; Suspect Liu Fulong Prosecuted

Shi Yuancai, a 44-year-old masseur from Yangzhou at the Qingquan Bathhouse at 516 Avenue Edward VII, and Liu Fulong, 26 years old, had a dispute over a bar of soap at around 5:00 PM the day before yesterday. The dispute escalated into a physical altercation, resulting in Shi being injured in the waist. Another companion, Qian Laosan, took Shi to the Yongfa Warehouse in the French Concession to rest. At 11:00 PM, his condition worsened, and Qian transported him to Renji Hospital, where he died despite treatment. The hospital reported the death to the Laozha Police Station, which dispatched detective Chen Ruisheng to investigate. Liu was arrested and taken to the police station for detention. The body was taken to the Forensic Examination Office on Avenue Foch. Yesterday morning, Guo Wei, a prosecutor from the First Special District Court, accompanied by forensic doctors Wei and Zhang, and court clerk Wang Zuyi, arrived at the morgue to examine the body. According to the report of Chinese police chief Lu Dagong, Liu Fulong had already been sent to the court and a postponement had been approved. Zhang Wancai, 30 years old, who also worked as a masseur at the bathhouse, reported that Liu was giving a rubdown to a customer who had brought his own bar of soap. Shi took the soap to use, which displeased the customer. Liu then asked Shi to return the soap, but Shi refused, leading to the dispute. He saw Shi push Liu first, and Liu retaliated with a punch to his waist. After being separated, Shi was still able to continue working. When questioned, Liu Fulong admitted to the physical altercation. Guo concluded that the deceased, Shi Yuancai, male, died of a ruptured spleen caused by the injury. The suspect, Liu Fulong, should be prosecuted by the police according to law and sent to the court for review. The body was handed over to Pushan Cemetery for burial.

Another Confiscation of Illegally Exported Silver Dollars

Since the Ministry of Finance of the National Government promulgated the temporary regulations prohibiting the export of silver on July 15th of this year, Customs inspectors have repeatedly seized cases of smuggling. The amounts range from two or three hundred yuan to as little as several tens of yuan. The perpetrators have been sentenced to imprisonment for three or four years or one or two years by the local court. Yesterday, Customs inspectors on a foreign warship (bound for Hong Kong) in Wusong discovered that Tan Shiquan (26 years old, from Guangdong) was carrying a large sum of silver dollars, totaling 2,700 yuan (Tan was selling groceries on the ship), with the intention of smuggling them out for profit. The Customs inspectors notified the Water Police Station, who sent police to board the ship and arrest Tan for interrogation at the local court. The 2,700 silver dollars were taken back to the Customs for confiscation.

Gambling and Opium Den Broken Up in Juelu Hotel: Proprietor and Gamblers Arrested; Many Opium Pipes and Paste Seized

Liu Yaying and Lu Dagong, Chinese police chiefs from the Laozha Police Station, recently learned that Rooms 108 and 82 of the Juelu Hotel at No. 250 Xizang Road were being used to organize large-scale opium sales and gambling dens. They began an investigation and learned that the operation was run by Ji Zengshou, a well-known gangster nicknamed "Little Marketplace Cake," and that the scale was very large. On the 12th of this month, they led detectives Wang Jiaju and Pang Yutang to raid the hotel. They arrested the proprietors, Hong Longsheng and Ji Zengshou from Suzhou, and the mahjong players Gu Bin, Li Jinsheng, Shan Kuanxian, and Chen Ahua in Room 108. They confiscated 145 yuan in gambling money, many chips, and arrested the gambling den employees Zhou Fusheng and Zhu Apei, as well as spectators Wu Meisheng, Hu Yaoxuan, Zhu Wanwen, Li Genfa, Cao Jinsheng, Wu Youwen, and Wang Sheng. In Room 82, they arrested Zhang Xiaoli for selling opium. Underneath a chair seat and the floor, they seized many opium pipes, opium paraphernalia, opium paste, and accounting books. The Juelu Hotel employee Zhang Ronggen testified that the gambling and opium den was opened by Hong Longsheng and Ji Zengshou and provided a written statement. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the First Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Police Lawyer Wang Yaotang explained the circumstances, and charged them under Articles 266 and 268 of the Criminal Code and Articles 6 and 11 of the Anti-Opium Law. He stated that besides Gu Bin, Li Jinsheng, Shan Binxian, and Chen Ahua, who were gambling, the rest were spectators. However, the police believed that the other suspects were there to smoke opium and that there was evidence of both gambling and opium use for investigation. Liu, the police chief, reported the details of the raid. Zhang Ronggen, a Juelu Hotel employee, suddenly overturned his previous statement, claiming that Ji Zengshou had nothing to do with the two rooms, seemingly out of fear. When questioned, Hong Longsheng admitted that he set up the gambling den, but Ji Zengshou firmly denied it. After questioning by Judge Qian Hongye, the case was adjourned for one week. Hong Longsheng, Ji Zengshou, Zhang Xiaoli, Zhou Fusheng, and Zhu Apei were remanded in custody, and the rest were released on bail of 100 yuan each.

Industrial Testing Laboratory's Invention: Scientific Gypsum Copper Plating Method Achieves Success

Ordinary electroplating is mostly limited to metallic substances, and electroplating of non-metallic substances is still rare. Years ago, German scholars' research results made electroplating of non-metallic insulators a growing reality, becoming one of the latest scientific inventions. After several months of research by the Central Industrial Testing Laboratory of the Ministry of Industry, considerable progress has been made, and the copper plating of gypsum models has been completely successful. At the request of the Health Testing Department of the Executive Yuan, three copper-plated gypsum models were produced on behalf of the department, which were no different from those purchased by the department from Germany. The laboratory is currently continuing research on copper and gold and silver plating on paper, cloth, bone, wood, porcelain, leather, glass, etc., which is expected to be successful. At the same time, in order to meet social needs, the laboratory is now starting to undertake gypsum copper plating work entrusted by various parties.

Penalty Rules for Ships Evading Taxes in This City: All Ship Owners Should Pay Special Attention

In view of the fact that this year's ship owners often take advantage of the vast river area in this city and the difficulty in investigation, and often falsely report departures to evade taxes, the Finance Bureau of this city has specially ordered all ship tax offices to notify each other of the ship numbers applying for departure, distribute them to various inspectors for strict investigation, and reach an agreement with the Public Utilities Bureau. In the future, for ships canceling leave, the various ship offices must check the customs registration book for civil ships to find out whether there are any false reports of departure and entry. If there are any false reports of tax evasion, once verified, in addition to making up for the evaded taxes, a heavier penalty will be imposed in accordance with the regulations in order to maintain tax collection. It is reported that last month, the Shanghai South Ship Tax Office discovered more than 20 ships falsely reporting departure on the Longhua River and imposed penalties in accordance with the regulations. Now that ship owners see that the ship tax office's inspection is very strict, those who applied for leave last month but have not yet left this month mostly take the initiative to the shipping office to return the cargo ship license, or register with the ship tax office and pay taxes with the cargo ship license retention certificate to avoid being discovered and penalized by the ship tax office. The relevant clauses of the bureau's rules on penalties for ships violating regulations are attached below for reference by all ship owners in this city. "Article 5": If a ship that has been inspected but has evaded taxes is found, in addition to being ordered to pay the monthly tax for the current term and making up for the evaded taxes in accordance with Article 8 of the Detailed Rules for the Collection of Ship Taxes, the following fines will be imposed according to the grade: (A) Those who have evaded taxes for more than one month shall be fined half of the monthly tax payable; (B) Those who have evaded taxes for more than two months shall be fined the amount of one month's tax payable; (C) Those who have evaded taxes for more than six months shall be fined twice the amount of one month's tax payable; (D) Those who have evaded taxes for more than nine months shall be fined three times the amount of one month's tax payable. "Article 6" Whoever falsely reports departure but still sails in the rivers of this city and intentionally evades taxes, in addition to being handled in accordance with Article 5, shall be subject to an additional fine of one month's tax.

Lu Xihou Sued for Fraud Continues to Be Heard; Lu Zutong Surrenders Himself Yesterday; Clarifying the Discounting Process of Promissory Notes

China and Foreign Bank has been closed for a year since the day after the Double Tenth Festival last year. The actual directors of the bank, Lu Xihou, manager Lu Mengxiang, and Sun Xiren, were arrested by the police station at the time and prosecuted by the First Special District District Court for crimes such as fraud, embezzlement, and breach of trust. Later, because the two Lu applied to declare the bank bankrupt, this criminal lawsuit was temporarily suspended. Recently, all civil matters have been resolved by the court one after another, so the public prosecution previously filed by the police station was reheard by Judge Qian Hongye. However, when the civil court

was conducting the trial, it was discovered that the bank had issued three promissory notes, each worth 5,000 yuan, on October 1 last year, all dated October 11 of the same month, and discounted them at the Kunshan and Suzhou branches of Ningbo Industrial Bank before they expired. After the bank closed, Wu Zhihao, the general manager of Ningbo Industrial Bank, ordered Lu Zutong, the manager of the Kunshan branch, to represent them in suing Lu Xihou and others to the First Special Court. Later, an out-of-court settlement was reached. Ningbo Industrial Bank believed that it had priority over the discounted funds and could not be treated the same as ordinary creditors, so it

did not suffer losses. After the accountant verified this situation, he reported the facts truthfully, causing the police station to determine that Lu Zutong was suspected of colluding with Lu Xihou and others to obtain illegal benefits, causing other creditors to suffer unexpected losses. Therefore, a lawsuit for fraud was also filed against Lu Zutong. The court session was held last week, but Zutong failed to appear after being summoned, and the trial was postponed. The details have been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Qian continued the joint interrogation. Lu Zutong surrendered himself with his defense lawyers Wu Peng and Lu Qi. The others, Lu Xihou, Lu Mengxiang, and Sun Xiren, also attended the court with their defense lawyers Wu Lindi and Fan Gang. Lawyer Ru Baoyi of the police station

stated the prosecution. After questioning Zutong about the case, he requested that Qi Shengfeng, a staff member of Talley & Company who was present in court, be questioned first about the transfer of the title deed at that time regarding Lu Xihou's wife, Wang, using a title deed to entrust it to the China Industrial Bank and then being mortgaged by the bank to the Siming Bank. The court then read it to Qi once, and then lawyer Wu Goukun explained in detail the reason for the repeated mortgage of the title deed, supplementing the lack of Lu Xihou's confession, saying that Lu borrowed the title deed from his wife because the bank needed funds, but he did not want the bank to be known as a lender, so he ordered his wife to

mortgage a title deed to the bank's business department for 70,000 yuan, and then deposit the funds in the savings department. The bank then used the title deed as collateral for receiving banknotes from Siming Bank. Later, Lu did not want to make those related to him, such as Daqian World, etc., owe the bank money, so he took out 70,000 yuan from his wife's savings department to repay the debts. The court then asked the defendant Lu Zutong to study the discounting process. According to his confession, on October 1 last year, Wu from China Industrial Bank negotiated the discounting of three promissory notes. I discounted two of them at the Kunshan branch of Ningbo Industrial Bank, totaling 10,000 yuan. The remaining one, worth 5,000 yuan, was discounted by Wu at the Suzhou branch. Wu

stated verbally that the rent of the building of China and Foreign Bank was used as a guarantee for the promissory note. Later, before the note expired, the bank had closed. General Manager Wu Zhihao transferred one of the notes collected by the Suzhou branch to me and sued Lu Xihou and others. The court verified the confession and said that according to the accountant's report, one note worth 5,000 yuan had already been cashed by China Industrial Bank, so the confession may not be true. He said that there was no need to hide it and that he should confess quickly to avoid being punished. He also questioned the defendant Lu Mengxiang about the issuance of the promissory notes, and then ordered the debate to begin, but it was too late, and the lawyers did not have time to finish their speeches. The bell rang five times, and Judge Qian ordered that the hearing be continued next Wednesday afternoon. Lu Zutong was released on bail or collateral with 1,000 yuan in cash.

French Concession: Baoyu Lane Rent Reduced by 10%

The houses in Baoyu Lane and the surrounding area on East Xinqiao Street and Avenue Edward VII in the French Concession are properties of the Renji Hospital, managed by the Dehe Foreign Firm. Since the economic downturn, many tenants in these houses have moved out, causing the sub-landlords to complain incessantly. The tenants requested the landlords to reduce the rent, and the landlords, understanding the current economic situation, accepted the tenants' request. After negotiations, it has been uniformly decided to reduce the rent by 10% to ease the burden on the tenants. Starting this month, all tenants will pay their rent at a 10% discount from the original amount.

Robbery by Throwing Pepper Powder; Thief Chen Zhaoyuan Sentenced to Three Years

Zhu Wu, a woman from Anhui residing at No. 31 Chengyu Lane, Lafayette Road, was instructed by her husband, Zhu Jiuhui, on August 26th, to withdraw 1,200 yuan in cash from the Guangda Pawnshop on Rue Bayle for use. She wrapped the banknotes in newspaper and held them in her hand on her way home. When she reached outside the back door of No. 28 Chengyu Lane, she was suddenly attacked by two male and one female robbers who threw pepper powder into her eyes, snatched the banknote package, and fled. She shouted for help while injured and chased the robbers to Fangxie Road in the Chinese area. The robbers opened fire along the way to resist capture. Police detectives intercepted a robber named Chen Zhaoyuan (44 years old) from Jingjiang, and confiscated 195 yuan. The French police handed him over to the Special Court for prosecution. According to Chen's confession during interrogation, he was instigated by Tang Xueting, a former military officer who is still at large, to commit the robbery. The victim, Zhu Wu, filed a collateral private lawsuit seeking to recover the stolen money. The case has been concluded and the date for sentencing has been set, as reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Neng Hui-ping presided over the First Criminal Division and sentenced Chen Zhaoyuan to three years of imprisonment for armed robbery with accomplices, and ordered him to compensate Zhu Wu with 1,006 yuan. After the sentencing, it was known that the defendant was to be notified to the Shanghai Public Safety Bureau to be apprehended and tried for injuring people by firing a gun in the Chinese territory, and temporarily detained in the detention center pending instructions.

Private Chop Forgery: Swindling Four Bicycles; Zhang Yifang Masterminds and Flees, Chen Fuliang and Xu Adi Arrested

Song Linfu, a native of Nantong, runs a bicycle shop named Linfu Bicycle Shop at No. 2098 Route Higer. Song is friendly with Huang Jin-xing, a Guangdong native residing at No. 18 Xitai Lane, Shenjiazhai. A friend of Huang's named Zhang Yifang often visits Huang's house and sometimes eats at the same table, and Song Linfu knows him well. The day before yesterday morning, Zhang, holding a guarantee slip stamped with Wang Jin-xing's seal, went to Song's shop with four other people and rented four bicycles, stating that they would return them at 3:00 PM. Song, seeing that they were acquaintances, did not doubt them and did not carefully examine the Wang and Huang characters on the guarantee slip. He handed over the four bicycles to the four men, who rode them away. After waiting until the next day without seeing them return, he went to Huang's house to inquire. Huang was completely unaware and denied having guaranteed the rental of any bicycles. While the two were wondering about this, one of the men who had come to rent the bicycles rode back to return one. Song immediately detained him, called the police, and sent him to the Xuhui Police Station. After interrogation by the station chief, the man confessed his name was Chen Fuliang, 16 years old, a Shanghai native residing at No. 9, Lane 78, Wuditou, and worked as a carpenter. He said that Zhang Yifang came up with the idea, knowing that Huang and Song were friendly and that he could rent bicycles with Huang's seal. He then discussed it with Xu Adi, a Songjiang native residing at No. 27 Triangle Ground who worked as a tailor. They went to a seal-engraving shop to privately engrave Wang Jin-xing's seal, wrote out a guarantee slip, and went to Song's shop to rent four bicycles. He rode one, and the others were ridden by Guo Zhangfang, 24 years old, a tailor residing at No. 18 Yinjiajiao, Shi Aqing, 17 years old, a carpenter residing at No. 11 Wuditou, and Shen Jingen, 17 years old, a carpenter residing at No. 1 Shenjiazhai. The three men each rode one to Songjiang. Because they had no money for food, they pawned one bicycle for eight yuan. The other two bicycles were taken away by Zhang Yifang. Fearing implication, he rode back to return the bicycle. After Chen's confession, the station chief ordered the police to arrest Guo, Shi, and Shen. Xu Adi was sent to the station by his father. Yesterday, all of them were sent to the Shanghai Public Safety Bureau for interrogation, and a strict search is underway for Zhang Yifang, who is still at large, to bring him to justice and recover the stolen bicycles.

Shaoxing Seven Counties Association Held Annual Meeting Yesterday

The Shanghai Association of natives from the seven counties of Shaoxing held its 25th annual members' meeting yesterday at 2:00 PM at its clubhouse on Avenue Albert. Mr. Zhu Xiaofan was elected chairman and the meeting proceeded with formalities. The chairman appointed Xu Xiajun, He Wuliang, Yao Jiafu, and Zhang Zheng-gang as ritual officers. The chairman then reported the purpose of the meeting, stating that according to the association's charter, the annual meeting should have been held on the 6th of this month, but due to work-related reasons, most of the natives were not in Shanghai at that time, so it was postponed to today. The association has been established for 25 years, but its affairs have not been fully developed, mainly because the natives have too shallow a view of the association. The number of people attending today's meeting is not large. During the National Games, it may be because the members have considerable faith in the association's staff and are too busy to spare time and are at ease with the association. Shrouded in an economic downturn, the backbone of our natives in Shanghai are mostly in the financial sector, and finance is the center of all industries. I believe that only struggle can break through this difficult situation, and only unity and mutual assistance can achieve the goal of struggle. The so-called "Heaven never cuts off all means of survival" can teach oneself, benefit fellow natives, and benefit society. At this gathering of our natives, we should encourage each other. This year is an election year. I hope that the committee members will work hard on the association's affairs, seek the welfare of the natives in Shanghai, and seek social order in the interior. With one heart and one mind, the whole, not divided, uses a new talent pool to develop new paths for the association. Then, Zheng Wentong reported on general affairs, Yan Chengde reported on financial affairs, and Shou Xiaotian reported on fundraising affairs. The Shanghai Municipal Party Committee representative Qian Youlan gave a speech, followed by discussions on: (1) Group insurance for members of the association, with members paying a small insurance fee each year, to negotiate with the China United Assurance Corporation in the name of the group. It was resolved in principle to pass the case. The execution committee will handle whether to designate China United Assurance Corporation and how to handle it. (2) For the convenience of insurance and native communication, another directory of members will be printed, detailing their name, age, occupation, address, etc. It was decided to handle it jointly with the first case. (3) Collect the association's original books and solicit publications from domestic agencies, bureaus, and schools to run a popular library for the benefit of the natives. It was decided that the executive committee will handle how to develop the association's original library within the possible scope of implementation. (4) Invite fellow natives from the banking industry to discuss developing hometown industries, such as improving papermaking, afforestation, and running a cement factory. It was decided to transfer it to the executive committee to consult with the banking industry and handle it as appropriate. (5) Propose soliciting member background information for record keeping. It was decided to carry out native registration and establish county group committees in each county to cooperate. (6) Propose increasing scholarships for children of the seven counties. It was decided to organize free registration for fellow natives, handle it in detail, and hand it over to the executive committee to handle. After the discussion, the results of the election of executive and supervisory committee members were announced: Wang Xiaolai, Pei Yunqing, Yan Chengde, Wang Yansong, Shou Xiaotian, Song Hantong, Xu Laijun, Xu Qianlin, Zhu Yaochen, Weng Yunhe, Zheng Wentong, Feng Zhongqing, Wei Qifang, Yuan Ludeng, Shen Jingke, Qi Ziquan, Wei Hongwen, Wei Shanfu, Yao Jiashi, Zhu Yun-san, Feng Meixue, Yu Qishan, Yuan Jinchu, Lu Zhinan, Huang Longchu, He Wuliang, Shen Jiuyu, He Eran, Tian Dafu, Xie Yunshou, and Shen Jinhuai were elected as executive committee members. Feng Yangyuan, Gao Peiliang, Shi Jiu'ao, Zhu Detian, Tong Xinbo, Shen Jinzhou, Hu Disheng, Lou Fengshao, and Zhao Weiren were elected as alternate executive committee members. Zhao Zichuan, Jiang Quanmao, Wang Juru, Shen Jinyong, Wu Guochang, Zhu Dingyi, Tian Qiyuan, Hu Chunxiang, Gu Wenchao, Xie Taofu, Shen Jian-san, Tian Xiangru, Lu Tingjian, Sun Jitang, and Xie Shaogeng were elected as supervisory committee members. Jin Jianqing, He Zhongxiao, Lu Zhengbing, Tao Baichuan, and Qi Yongqing were elected as alternate supervisory committee members. After the elections, a dinner was held. At the same time, Yue Opera performers from the Gongyu and Yuesheng troupes were invited to perform Yue Opera to add to the fun. Valuable gifts were distributed to commemorate the occasion. The event lasted until midnight and then everyone dispersed happily.

Chinese Buddhist Association: Expanding Organization and Seeking Members; From the First of This Month to December

The Chinese Buddhist Association has been established for seven years. Due to changes in the organizational system, the Buddhist county branches in all provinces and cities will be reorganized uniformly, and membership will be expanded. The solicitation period will run from the 1st of this month to the end of December. In addition to establishing a solicitation committee in the General Assembly, a general team will also be established to take charge of everything. It is learned that the association's chairman, Venerable Yuan Ying, during his spare time from lecturing on scriptures in Nanxiang every day, regularly attends the association to work.

Eight Major Fur Goods Stores Sell Off Stock at Low Prices

Hengruntai, Yuanshentai, Qinghexing, Qianfayuan, Tianqingfu, Qianfengtai, Dajicheng, and Tianfaxiang, eight major fur goods stores, recently sold off all the remaining stock of Zhengxiangtai and Lao Xiangtai at low prices, worth more than 220,000 yuan. They are now in the process of sorting and marking down the prices, selling them off at 10% to 50% of the original price. Items that used to sell for ten yuan at Zhengxiangtai and Lao Xiangtai are now selling for only one to five yuan. Each item is marked with the actual price, allowing customers to choose freely. This kind of low-price sale is truly a new record in the fur goods industry.

Hunan Renji Factory's Refined Pencil Lead Powder Sells Well; Purity Above 95 Degrees

Pencil lead powder is an essential raw material for manufacturing dry batteries. Domestic battery factories generally use imported goods, and the demand is quite large, costing over 500 yuan per ton, which is a major drain. Although Jiangsu also has this mineral product, it is not suitable for use due to its poor quality. The pencil lead powder refined by the Hunan Renji Industrial Raw Material Factory has a pure and good quality, with a purity above 95 degrees. Its efficacy is comparable to imported goods, but its price is less than half of the imported price. At present, battery factories in Guangdong and Guangxi, which used to use imported goods, are now happy to use the factory's products, and procurement is quite enthusiastic. It is reported that the factory's business office is located at No. 8 Xiahe Street, Changsha, Hunan. For Shanghai-related inquiries, please contact Mr. Wang Xingchu of Shishi Xinbao, Chang Geng Li, Avenue Edward VII, as representative.

Central Photo Studio Opens Branch at the Confucius Temple

The Central Photo Studio at Fangbang Bridge has been in business for many years and has a long history of service. The photographs taken are exceptionally clear. The photographers' skills are superb, personally guided by Mr. Qing Wu, so the products are excellent, and the prices are more modest than other businesses. As a result, the studio is crowded every day. Now, to promote convenience for customers, a branch has been established at the Confucius Temple. The natural scenery there is extremely elegant, so the photographers have also been very busy recently.

Yang Shaowei Goes to Japan to Study

Mr. Yang Shaowei has served in the military and tax circles and has made remarkable achievements. In order to seek further advancement, he is going to the Eastern Neighbor to concentrate on observing police administration and plans to study at the Higher Police Officer Training School. He took the Japanese mail ship Nagasaki Maru east on the 10th. Many fellow villagers, relatives, and friends went to see him off.

City Voices

Oriental Wireless Electric Insurance Company Offers Preferential Treatment to Customers

Since the Oriental Wireless Electric Insurance Company, located next to the East Silk Industry Bank on Shilu, Third Malu, expanded its internal operations, many people have enthusiastically insured their radios there. Most of these radios are often taken there for repairs due to sound insulation issues, and the repair fees are completely free of charge. Now, the company, after receiving letters from various sectors of society requesting amendments to the new regulations and extending the insurance period to six months for each contract, decided, after discussion, to adopt the premise of catering to the psychology of people in society and offering preferential treatment to customers. Regardless of whether they are already insured or not, all are subject to the new regulations. The new regulations stipulate that imported products are 6 yuan for six months, and domestic products are 3 yuan for six months. If there is any damage during the insurance period, all repairs and compensation are free. The telephone number is 96166. If it is inconvenient due to distance, you can call and they will arrive immediately.

Weather Report

Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:00 PM yesterday stated that the area around Shandong is sunny, and the wind direction will roughly turn north. This area and the middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River have rain, and the wind is from the east to southeast. There is fog in the coastal areas, and the Taiwan Strait is still clear and fine, with north to northeast winds. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the temperature in this port was a maximum of 81.5 and a minimum of 61.7. On the same day last year, the maximum was 84.2 and the minimum was 62.4.

Letters to the Editor

To the Editor,

Having read the news report on page 11 of section three of your newspaper dated October 14th regarding the negotiations for the capsized tugboat, the details stated are not consistent with the actual situation. In addition to the captain of the ship reporting the facts to the union, the driving aspect is afraid of confusing rumors, and a special letter is used to declare it. Sincerely request that you publish a letter in the corrections column, which is public sentiment. To the Editorial Department of Shen Bao, Shanghai Xiexing Shipping Transfer Company, 10/14

To the Editor,

I recently read a news item in today's edition of your newspaper regarding a conflict between members of the Wusong Defense Corps and a barber, which led to a barber strike. The facts are greatly inconsistent. On the afternoon of the 10th of this month, suddenly twenty to thirty rioters gathered on Taixing Road and fought each other. Police officer Ye Yousheng of the nearby (No. 1862) post attempted to stop them but was beaten. The police officer then frantically blew his whistle for help. Yang Zixiang, a squad leader in our corps, heard the sound and went forward to assist in the arrest, but was also violently beaten by the rioters, suffering head injuries and bleeding profusely. His military cap was also stolen. At the time, the ringleader Wang Shun-gao was apprehended, who confessed that he was invited by his sister-in-law, a barber, and other barbers to come and fight. Others who committed the assault and injured Squad Leader Yang include Wu Dahai, Wang Shunwen, Cao Jinshan, and three others whose names he could not remember. Other confessions were evasive. Subsequently, the Wusong Police Station apprehended both sides of the dispute and sent them to the judicial section for interrogation. Because our corps squad leader Yang Zixiang is in the position of the plaintiff, he is also one of the witnesses, so he also has to be brought to the case for questioning. As for the continued arrest of the suspects yesterday, the Yunzaobang Police Station has been consulted to assist in the matter, and there is nothing illegal to be said. Whether the strike is legitimate from a rational or emotional standpoint is not something our corps seems to be able to point out, but the facts are obviously inconsistent with what is stated in your newspaper. Since this concerns public opinion, we have specially prepared this letter to ask you to correct it. We hope you will take this into consideration. To the Editorial Department of Shen Bao Headquarters, Shanghai Wusong Defense Corps, 10/13
