Men's and Women's National Arts

Yu Wins Archery Championship; Men's Champion and Runner-Up Swept; Bullet Finals Held Today

The National Arts competition yesterday morning featured the men's and women's archery (long-range) finals, and the afternoon featured the men's and women's singles weapons preliminaries. The Mongolian wrestling team still came to the venue to observe and participate in friendly matches with wrestlers from Ping, Lu, and Hu. Chu Minyi performed the Tai Chi ball and stick, and all the programs were quite spectacular. Therefore, yesterday afternoon, the National Arts venue was particularly crowded. When the Mongolians wrestled with the Han people, there was a veritable crush of people. The results of each group competition and other details are described below:

Archery Competition Swept by Northerners

In the archery (long-range) competition held in the morning, the athletes from Yu Province showed their skills, sweeping the champion and runner-up in both the men's and women's groups. The champion in the women's group, Kou Fenglan, still wore her hair in a bun and dressed very simply. The Ma sisters, when drawing their bows and shooting arrows, glared fiercely with their eyes, truly embodying the spirit of female heroes. It is reported that their usual scores can reach over one hundred meters. Yesterday, they encountered headwinds, and because the wind was strong, their scores were reduced. The sound of sighs was quite audible. Wrestling female athlete Meng Jianli also participated in the archery competition yesterday, but she ranked fifth because she had exerted too much effort during the wrestling competition the day before, and her strength had not yet recovered. In the men's group, Jin Deshun, a Beiping athlete, had completely white hair, but his spirit was strong, truly proving that old age is full of vigor. One arrow was shot far, reaching over one hundred meters, winning third place. Overall, the archery competition was completely swept by northern athletes, with southerners having almost no chance to participate, which also shows the great difference between martial arts in southern and northern China.

Final Results of Women's Long-Range Archery

In the women's long-range archery final held in the morning, only representatives from Henan and Shanghai participated, totaling seven people. However, Chen Jinchai, No. 1979 from Shanghai, forfeited the competition, so only six people competed. Henan sent three female athletes: Ma Ruilian, Ma Ruilan, and Kou Fenglan. Shanghai sent three women: Meng Jianli, Zhao Jingfang, and Wang Jinxia. Ma Ruilan was first, shooting three consecutive arrows, all of which were far beyond the venue, exceeding the original distance, creating a new record for the competition, and causing all the spectators to be astonished. The four-time recorder and referee had to lengthen the distance standard line for calculation. After a busy time, Wang Jinxia and others continued the competition. Each person participated twice, with three arrows each time. The top two names were all won by the three female players from Henan. The results of the six people are listed below:

Chu Minyi Performs Tai Chi Ball

Chu Minyi performed Tai Chi Ball and Tai Chi Stick at the National Arts Venue at 4:00 PM yesterday. Wu Shanchang also came to visit and applauded non-stop. Chu wore beige clothes and pants and long black leather boots, looking energetic with developed muscles. The Tai Chi Ball was made of copper-plated nickel, about one foot in diameter, weighing thirty kilograms, and as bright as a mirror, suspended on a wooden frame. The Tai Chi Stick was a foot long and as thick as a small arm, attached to the frame by a rubber band. Chu first performed the Tai Chi Ball, frequently rubbing the ball with his back, chest, abdomen, and arms, and Chu's muscles also bulged one by one. The performance was quite spectacular. He then performed the Tai Chi Stick, with movements similar to the Tai Chi Ball, lasting about ten minutes.

Mongolian Wrestling Team Is Truly Powerful

After the Mongolian wrestling team arrived, they immediately conducted friendly matches with wrestling athletes from North China. The first pair was Aornasutu (Mongolian) against Wei Dehai (Ping). Wei was also tall and mighty. Once they began, Wei was immediately thrown to the ground by Aornasutu. The second pair was Batur (Mongolian) against Shan Shijun (Ping). Shan entering the venue seemed to have a special interest in this sport, so he danced and swayed when facing the Mongolian, expressing his joy. But once the two men met, Shan tried to grab Batur's collar, but the Mongolian wrestling clothes were made of leather with copper nails, so there was no way to grab them. Instead, Batur grabbed Shan's back and pushed him back, and Shan could not support himself and fell to the ground. The third pair was Badama (Mongolian) against Li Zhenqing (Hu), who also fell to the ground after a single attempt. At this time, veteran Bi Fengting could not stand the arrogance of the Mongolians, so he volunteered to step forward and fight the Mongolians to avenge the shame of the three previous defeats. The opponent was Buhe (Mongolian). With the sound of a whistle, Bi rushed forward to fight. They held each other for a long time, and Bi could still support himself, so the general audience applauded greatly. Unfortunately, the veteran was careless and was thrown to the ground by Buhe using brute force, and Bi retired in anger. The fourth pair was Samadaenzhamu (Mongolian) against Bu Enfu (Ji). Bu had a relatively slender lower body and knew that he could not win by strength, so he sought a different way to win. When the two men began, Bu took a defensive posture. But the Mongolian was as strong as an ox and grabbed Bu's sleeves, dragging Bu, who was almost in a dangerous situation. Fortunately, Bu was skilled in application and did not fall. Bu then waited for an opportunity to attack. At one point, Bu took advantage of the situation and grabbed Sama's sleeve, dragging him forward and butting Sama's chest with his head, while raising his right foot to hook Sama's left foot. Sama could not support himself and fell to the left, but Sama's strength was great, and he used this opportunity to press his entire body towards Bu. The two fell to the ground at the same time, and Bu, falling below, lost the battle. Afterwards, the players from various places stopped advancing. Although there were still two wrestling matches, they ultimately failed. The reason for the failure was not just lack of effort. The wrestling clothes worn by the Mongolians were specially made and difficult to grab, so it was difficult to use strength and difficult to apply techniques, which was the biggest reason for the failure.

Yesterday's Memorial Week Ceremony Led by Mayor Wu and Director Pan

Yesterday, Monday, the National Games Memorial Week was held at the gymnasium at 8:30 AM. Mayor Wu and Director Pan led the ceremony. Security team members, police officers, Boy Scouts, and athletes all participated. After the ceremony, Mayor Wu gave a speech, stating that it was not by chance that everyone was able to hold the Memorial Week here today but was a result of the well-planned and united Sixth National Games. The holding of this National Games allowed Shanghai's 3.5 million residents to witness dozens of physically and mentally vigorous athletes from various provinces, proving to the young people present that China's desire for a healthy population and a strong nation is not impossible. We must know that the current national difficulties and dangers were not created overnight but are the result of over a hundred years of weakness, leading to today's severe national crisis. Therefore, to ensure the nation's survival, we must continue to strive with a spirit of perseverance for a long-term revival. At this point, Mayor Wu cited the German nation before and after the European War and its current revival as evidence, encouraging the people to endure hardship and strive for national strength. However, the physical and mental strength of the nation depends on the people's training and promotion of sports. I sincerely hope that the athletes representing various provinces and cities in the National Games can become practitioners who spread the seeds of strong national work. The future strength of China and the foundation for national revival lie entirely in the actions of today's youth. I hereby offer this chapter as encouragement to all staff and athletes.

First Preparatory Meeting of the Chinese Physical Education Society

Continuing to solicit initiators, another meeting on the 17th

The Chinese Physical Education Society held its first preparatory meeting at the Deling Apartment yesterday. Yuan Dunli chaired the meeting and appointed Hao Gengsheng, Wu Yunrui, Cheng Dengke, Yuan Jiaoli, Shen Siliang, Shao Rugan, Wu Cheng, Zhang Dongping, Wu Bangwei, Wang Lianggui, and ten others to be responsible for the preparations and continue to solicit initiators. The solicitation letter has already been sent out and is recorded below: Dear Sir, Physical education in our country has made significant progress in recent years due to the active promotion by the whole country. However, the driving force behind its promotion is mostly focused on administration, teaching, and competition, and there is still a lack of purely academic research institutions for physical education, resulting in little discussion of practical theories in physical education. The Qingdao Physical Education Discussion Group of the Chinese Physical Education Association and colleagues in the education field in Beijing and Shanghai, in view of this, have proposed the organization of the Chinese Physical Education Society to provide opportunities for the dissemination and research of physical education. The first preparatory meeting was held at Deling Apartment at 6:00 PM on the 13th of this month. It was unanimously agreed to take advantage of the Sixth National Games in Shanghai, where leaders and celebrities from the national youth education sector are gathered, to solicit initiators to facilitate the process, and it was decided that the initiators' meeting will be held again at 6:00 PM on the 17th of this month in the dining room on the second floor of Deling Apartment on Sichuan Road. We have always admired your enthusiasm for physical education and your leadership among the masses. We respectfully hope that you will grant us your permission to attend the meeting on time.

Random Notes from the Gymnasium

New Additions to the Gymnasium:

A new addition to the gymnasium is a large wireless broadcasting machine. There are sub-machines inside and outside the gymnasium. One moment it's Peking opera, the next it's songs, which is quite lively. However, during the competition, it feels a bit obtrusive. Its sound mixes with the referee's whistle, which can cause confusion. Later, it was temporarily stopped and only broadcast during breaks or after each match.

Various Different Roars:

The competition has been tense for days, and each team has organized cheering squads that cheer loudly. The sounds made by the men are sometimes like Tarzan's roar, and sometimes like the roar of King Kong in the King Kong movie. The sounds made by the women are like echoes from warships or factories, and sometimes like the roar of lions. If these various sounds were sometimes recorded, they could become a spectacle of strange sounds.

Beautiful Costumes:

The costumes of the Shanghai and Malayan women's basketball players are extremely beautiful. Shanghai's are yellow silk shirts with red characters and purple pants, with strong colors. The Malayan team has peach-colored shirts and snow-white pants, with jade arms fully exposed, with bright colors. During the competition, it's like colorful butterflies flying, and like heavenly maidens scattering flowers. Several ladies and young ladies said softly, "What beautiful costumes!"

Identification by Hair:

In the women's basketball game between Guangdong and Qingdao the day before yesterday, all the Guangdong girls had permed hair, while the Qingdao girls did not. Therefore, the referee felt it was very convenient. When officiating, there was no need to look at the team names on the teams' uniforms, as they could be identified by their hair.

"Can't Run, Brother!"

The basketball court in the gymnasium is extremely well-constructed, and the ground is exceptionally smooth. Most athletes from the interior have never been to such a venue. In addition, their skills are also poor, so they often somersault and fall with every step, as if they were climbing an oiled mountain, with a sigh of "Can't run, brother!"

Betting Two Chicken Cakes:

In the battle between Qingdao and Malaya, two spectators bet on the winner. One bought a ticket for Qingdao, and the other bought a ticket for Malaya. The item they were betting on was two large chicken cakes. As a result, the one who bet on Qingdao won. The one who bet on Malaya had to rub his belly and go hungry.

Meeting of Representatives of the Jiangsu Provincial Secondary School Faculty and Staff Association

The 17th Congress of Representatives of the Jiangsu Provincial Secondary School Faculty and Staff Association was held at the Provincial Shanghai Middle School on the 9th. Chen Zhenbai chaired the meeting. The following were elected as directors: Huang Boqin (18 votes), Zhang Zhonghuan (19 votes), Rong Weisheng (17 votes), Wu Cangsu (15 votes), Zhang Tongmo (15 votes), Zhang Shaonan (14 votes), Xu Chongde (10 votes), Zhang Songnian (13 votes), Wu Zonghan (13 votes). The above nine people were elected as directors. Xue Xialing (9 votes), Gao Shiguang (8 votes), He Daomin (8 votes). The above three people were elected as alternate directors. Huang Boqin was elected as chairman by the directors. Discussion of proposals: A. Administrative Inspection Category 1. The method of combining education, training, and military affairs in each school is in the trial implementation period, and the implementation situation is difficult to unify. Should the association convene the persons in charge of education, training, and military affairs of each school to discuss the progress in accordance with the previous academic conference method? Resolved: Passed. 2. Students with excellent graduation examination results from normal schools should be specially approved by the Department of Education to shorten the service period to two years, and they should be given rewards and assistance in accordance with the method of rewarding ordinary high school students to facilitate further study. Resolved: Passed. 3. Request the Department of Education to improve the supervision and guidance methods and to deal with the punishment of faculty and staff of provincial schools with caution. Resolved: (A) In the future, the Department of Education should focus on active guidance for supervision and inspection. (B) Supervisors should be filled by those with specialized academic qualifications and rich secondary school teaching experience. (C) The inspection of teaching status should adopt a departmental system, with one supervisor assigned to each subject. (D) Increase the inspection time, with each subject requiring at least one unit of inspection. (E) Differences in the situation of each school are inevitable. Supervisors should first inquire with the school when they have questions. (F) When necessary, supervisors should accept the teacher's request to conduct demonstration teaching. (G) After receiving the inspection report, the Department of Education should consult with the school on the important points and order them to submit a reply. Please do not make rewards and punishments based solely on one-sided reports. (H) Please do not disclose reward and punishment matters in newspapers. 4. How should the association express itself regarding the case of Mr. Yang Yinmin, a member of the association? Resolved: 1. Request the Department of Education to conduct a thorough investigation and make a fair decision. 2. Send a telegram of condolence to Yang. B. Curriculum and Teaching Materials Category 1. There are many discrepancies between the curriculum standards issued by the Ministry of Education and the progress schedule set by the Department. How should the situation be remedied? Resolved: Submit to the Department of Education for instructions. 2. Request the Department of Education to publish the standard answers to the questions for the joint examination. Resolved: Passed. Send a letter to the school federation to forward to the Department of Education. 3. After the reform of normal schools, there has been no special textbook for subjects such as arithmetic, physics, chemistry, history, and geography. High school textbooks are mostly used as substitutes, and both quality and quantity are felt to be inadequate. If teachers compile their own handouts, it will be difficult to ensure consistency in the amount of teaching materials among schools. It should be requested that the Department of Education forward the request to the Ministry of Education to promptly compile and print textbooks so that the effectiveness of the curriculum standards can be fully utilized for teaching. Resolved: Passed. 4. The high school and junior high school textbooks printed by the Middle School Bookstore are compiled in accordance with the progress schedule issued by the Department. Each school should adopt them, but these textbooks have not yet been approved by the Ministry of Education, which is a violation of the Ministry's orders. It should be requested that the Department of Education order the bookstore to promptly submit them to the Ministry for review. Resolved: Passed. C. Further Education and Treatment Category 1. Please have the Department of Education implement Article 123 of the revised secondary school regulations promulgated by the Ministry of Education, which states that "secondary school teachers who have worked continuously in the same school for nine years may take a one-year sabbatical for research and investigation. 2. Request the Department of Education to send staff to visit domestic and foreign countries. Resolved: Passed. 3. Request the Department of Education to forward to the Ministry of Education to find ways to improve the summer teacher training classes and to carefully select lecturers to benefit colleagues. Resolved: Passed. 4. Request the Department of Education to issue an order to all schools to earnestly promote the full-time teacher system to increase teaching effectiveness. Resolved: Passed. 5. Request the Department of Education to strictly formulate teacher protection measures and earnestly implement them to stabilize teachers' academic interests and benefit the development of teaching. Resolved: Changed to "Request the Department of Education to strictly order all schools to comply with the regulations promulgated by the Ministry of Education regarding the term of employment contracts for teachers, with the initial appointment being one year and the renewal being two years." Resolved: Passed. D. Other 1. Cases resolved by previous congresses of representatives that have not been implemented should be handled promptly by the Board of Directors to facilitate the affairs of the association. Resolved: Passed. 2. Although the proposal to designate June 6 as Teachers' Day has been submitted, it has not yet been approved. It should still be requested that the Department of Education forward the request to the Ministry of Education to clearly designate it. Resolved: Passed. 3. Re-election of representatives to the Education Fee Committee. Resolved: The chairman will represent. 4. Determine the location of the next congress. Resolved: Yixing.

International Education Society Holds School Achievement Exhibition

This port is an area where Chinese and foreigners live together. People from all countries have established schools separately for the sake of educating their children. Their curriculum, academic system, teaching inspection, management, etc. are different from each other. Leaders in the education field, in view of this, organized the International Education Society in 1931, bringing educators from various countries together to study the improvement of school education. The presidents over the years have been Li Zhaohuan, president of Jiaotong University, Kang Xia, principal of Huatong Public School, and Wei Yusi, principal of the American School. Until 1937, when the election was changed, Dr. Wei Quegong was elected as president. The daily affairs of the society are to visit each other's schools, hold lectures and discuss educational issues on a regular basis. However, this year, in order to arouse the interest of all sectors of society in studying education, Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Shanghai Education Bureau, Hilliard, Director of the Department of Education of the Public Works Department, and Guo Sibo, Principal of the French School, were appointed as instructors, and it was decided to hold a large exhibition of the achievements of Chinese and Western schools at the Chinese Youth Association in Baxianqiao, French Concession from November 8 to 10 this year. In addition to displaying the achievements of Chinese and Western schools and giving speeches and writing competitions, students from each school will also arrange entertainment programs on a daily basis to entertain guests. The society has now appointed a committee to plan in various ways, and the work is very tense. Those who want to know the details of the academic exhibition can directly contact Mr. Baer of Mellon Middle School on Zhaofeng Road.

The Problem of Study Load and Teaching Time for Middle School Students (II)

-- Yi Ping

Leaving aside erroneous observations and inferences, let us conduct a vertical and horizontal examination of middle school teaching hours. First, regarding the vertical aspect, ten years before the founding of the Republic of China, that is, in the 28th year of the Guangxu reign of the Qing Dynasty, the Ministry of Education stipulated that the teaching hours for each subject in middle school were 36 hours per week. In the first year of the Republic of China, the Ministry of Education stipulated that the first year of boys' middle school was 33 hours, the second year was 34 hours, and the third and fourth years were each 35 hours. The number of hours for each grade in girls' middle school was reduced by one hour compared to the corresponding grade in boys' middle school, that is, from 32 to 34 hours. In the 18th year, the Ministry of Education of the National Government promulgated the Provisional Curriculum Standards, stipulating that the junior high school should have one hundred and eighty-six credits and the senior high school should have one hundred and fifty-six credits. On average, junior high school has 31 credits per semester and senior high school has 26 credits. At that time, the definition of a credit was: one hour of class per week per semester is one credit. However, drawing, crafts, music, physical education, and natural science experiments, as well as outside-of-class preparation, self-study, or preparation and self-study time that is relatively short, should be discounted. Therefore, in fact, 31 credits are at least 35 or 36 hours per week, and 26 credits are at least 33 or 34 hours per week, because senior high school has more natural science credits. Second, regarding the horizontal aspect, among the major European countries, France and Italy have relatively few teaching hours in middle school. According to the middle school teaching hours table implemented in France in April 1931, the second grade has 20 hours per week, the third to sixth grades have at least 12 hours per week and at most 23.5 hours per week, the seventh grade philosophy class has 24 hours, and the mathematics class has 25 hours. However, physical education and class discussions that occur in the classroom are not included in these hours. In Italy, middle school in the Ginnaio section has 21 hours per week in each grade, 24 hours per week in grades one to five, and 26 hours per week in grades one to three in the Liceo section. The science middle school in the Liceo section has 25 hours per week in the first grade and 26 hours per week in grades two to four. As with France, physical education hours are not included. Germany is a hardworking country. In the old various middle schools, the sixth and fifth grades of the classical middle school and the literary and practical middle school, that is, the first and second grades, each have 24 hours per week, and the fourth grade to the upper grade, that is, the third grade to the ninth grade, each have 26 to 28 hours per week. The sixth to fourth grades of the practical middle school, the new literary and practical middle school, and the German middle school each have 25 hours, and the lower two grades to the upper grade each have 26 to 28 hours. The newly established middle school after the European War is a six-year middle school from the lower three grades to the upper grade, with each grade having at least 28 hours per week and at most 30 hours, averaging 29 hours. None of the middle schools include physical education hours. Russia is a tough country. The first three years of her middle school continue the unified labor school and are called the fifth, sixth, and seventh grades. The fifth grade has 35 hours per week, and the sixth and seventh grades each have 36 hours. The last two years are called the eighth and ninth grades, and are divided into teacher training, cooperation, administration, and other departments. Each department is divided into groups. Except for three or several groups that have 36 or 37 hours per week, the rest each have 38 hours. This number includes physical education hours. The British middle school system is very inconsistent, but the British Ministry of Education has issued an order stating that middle schools that accept students aged 12 to 16 can adopt the teaching subjects and hours proposed by the Ministry. This table stipulates that teaching is 35 to 37 hours per week (to be continued).

Supplement to the Shanghai Shen Bao

Health and Medical Journal

A Few Words on Various Treatments for Gonorrhea

-- Dr. Yuan Yimin

There are so many drugs for treating gonorrhea and electrical machines for treating gonorrhea. Generally speaking, there are only four types of treatment: 1. Electrical therapy. The meaning of electrical therapy is to kill bacteria with heat, the so-called hyperthermia sterilization. Among these electrical therapies, only the short-wave diathermy machine is the most valuable. Those who use the Fulco motor and long-wave diathermy machine are difficult to achieve considerable results, and even extend the healing period. Moreover, they also have the drawbacks of burning the skin. In addition, in the acute urethral gonorrhea, irradiation with cold light from a mercury quartz lamp, the so-called light sterilization, also has considerable effect. 2. Injection therapy. Pigments and mixed gonorrhea vaccines are used alternately, one to kill bacteria with drugs and the other to automatically immunize, which can be said to be appropriate. 3. Internal thigh method. A special preparation with strong penetration, anti-inflammatory, bactericidal, and analgesic effects should be selected. The "Mesalym" of the German Merck Chemical Company can be said to be perfect in these aspects. 4. Local therapy. Usually, silver protein and other substances are used for washing and injecting, which is a direct drug sterilization method. If the time and concentration of the liquid are not appropriate, it will be laborious and ineffective, and it is not as effective as the direct immune method of the vaccine. "Gonorrhoea Relief," produced by the German Manerzda Pharmaceutical Factory, is a preparation of gonorrhea serum and relief, and is a special agent for treating urethral gonorrhea. It is now sold by the Ren Shou Western Drug Company in this port. Differences Between Sexual Neurasthenia and Cerebral Neurasthenia

— Physician Cui Fuqing

Sexual neurasthenia is a weakening disease of the nerves in the sexual organs. This means the sexual nerves are easily excited and easily fatigued, leading to reproductive organ dysfunction such as impotence or infertility. Prominent symptoms include spermatorrhea, premature ejaculation, and erectile dysfunction. The root cause is often excessive sexual activity and masturbation.

Cerebral neurasthenia is a symptom of general neurasthenia, most noticeably in the brain. Common symptoms include a feeling of pressure and heaviness in the head, sluggish thinking, poor memory, dizziness, blurred vision, indigestion, palpitations, insomnia, back pain, and weakness in the limbs. These symptoms gradually develop and affect the entire body, representing the most severe stage of neurasthenia. The causes are varied; aggravated sexual neurasthenia or excessive mental work can both lead to cerebral neurasthenia. Having sexual neurasthenia does not necessarily mean also having cerebral neurasthenia, but having cerebral neurasthenia often accompanies sexual neurasthenia. Regardless of whether it is cerebral or sexual neurasthenia, the underlying cause is nerve weakness, a deficiency of phosphorus and endocrine fluids in the body, which prevents proper nourishment of various organs. Therefore, taking reliable phosphorus and endocrine preparations can help. For example, "An Er Shen," sold by "Ren Shou Pharmacy," contains sufficient phosphorus and endocrine substances and is a specialized remedy for neurasthenia. Taking it as directed will yield good results. Talks

An Appeal to the National Games

— Xing An

The Sixth National Games opened on National Day at the city's stadium. This year, 38 units from various regions participated, with over 2,000 athletes, a new record for the Games. On that day, there were over 100,000 Chinese and foreign spectators, presenting an unprecedentedly enthusiastic scene. This shows that the Chinese people have a considerable understanding of sports. Our country has long been mocked as the "Sick Man of East Asia." If the Chinese people can uphold the belief of strengthening the country and the race, and everyone dedicates themselves to physical training, then the nation's future may still have hope for revival.

However, we feel that there are still some shortcomings and errors in our country's promotion of sports. Originally, the goal of promoting sports is to guide the people's physical health. To achieve this goal, we must strive to popularize sports so that all citizens, regardless of gender, age, or status, understand the importance of sports and practice beneficial exercises. However, our country's promotion of sports often neglects this. Previously, only schools had sports subjects. Although we have gradually paid attention to mass sports in recent years, it is still limited to a portion of the population and cannot be called popularization. The majority of the people still do not have the opportunity to participate in sports. This must be said to be a major shortcoming.

Furthermore, since the purpose of promoting sports is to strengthen the body, we cannot merely use winning medals as an incentive. The purpose of holding sports meets is to give athletes the opportunity to showcase their athletic skills and to arouse people's attention to sports. At a sports meet, we certainly hope to achieve excellent results. However, if we simply encourage athletes to compete for medals, this will only cultivate a few athletes and create a few records, which inevitably loses the true meaning of sports. Chinese athletes often exercise to show off. Furthermore, schools often promote sports to advertise the school. This attitude is very wrong.

We believe that the above two points need to be corrected. Therefore, as this National Games is being held, we are specifically raising these points for discussion. We hope that a group of patriotic people who are enthusiastic about sports will pay attention.

Grapes

— Yueshan

A friend from the dormitory gave me a branch of grapes, with two leaves still attached. Although the leaves were half-withered, they made the clusters of round pearls look very lovely. I did not eat them; I hung them by the lampshade on the desk corner, and the room suddenly became more colorful and harmonious. The green lampshade cast a yellowish-green light, which softly shone on the round pearls, making them even more adorable.

The grapes reminded me of a friend who used to steal grapes with me. That friend disappeared with the fall of the Northeast and has been separated from me for three years without any news.

Three years ago, we were studying at a church school on a hillside. Next to the school was a large orchard, planted with grapes all over the hill, which were used for winemaking. I had seen the servants carrying barrels of grapes to the kitchen to make wine. The foreign priest in a black gown, with a flushed face, spoke fluent Chinese and taught the servants what to do; the barrels of grapes smiled at us like pearls, but we students could not eat even one. Because the orchard was the residence of the priests, we could not enter.

But after I had that friend, that companion who stole grapes with me, I often ate grapes. I was afraid that only the two of us in the whole school were breaking the rules: climbing over the short wall, squatting under the grape trellis, tiptoeing to eat our fill, and often carrying out a big bag.

"Let's go," he didn't say much, just one word. The rough red face of that Northeasterner naturally revealed a few smiles, with a knowing look in his eyes. We would silently leave the dormitory, bypass the big pine forest, and walk towards the orchard. He always invited me. He was bold and smiled, and his smile was full of confidence, which made me not forget him. He was tall and had a lot of brute strength. He was not afraid of the servants who were loyal to the foreign masters; he often scolded them, calling them foreign dogs.

In the orchard, we were once caught by a servant. The servant was very kind and did not embarrass us, only gently saying, "Mr. Han, the priest is over there in the pavilion."

Mr. Han ignored him. I watched the servant's back fade away, feeling a little scared. I said, "Let's go, this big bag is enough for them to eat."

"Ignore him, what the x priest!" He was so overbearing, still turning his face away to pick grapes, those lovely round pearls.

After a while, a foreigner in a black robe appeared by the grape trellis. The round pearls turned into the priest's terrifying face. I looked up from below: a pair of long, shiny black leather shoes; above that: a black satin robe swaying in the wind; above that, above the round pearls, was a terrifying face, angry eyes, shooting out the fierce light of a beast. I was dumbfounded, because I remembered we had met him more than once.

Old Han tugged at the hem of my long gown, and I followed him away. The orchard was very quiet, and the green leaves were covered with the light of dusk.

"Hey, you!" the old priest said, chasing after us, calling us to stop. We stopped. Naturally, we received a lecture. The old priest also said some deceptive things about how everyone could eat when they were all ripe, saying that it was a private residence and we should not enter casually, and that entering and picking grapes was stealing.

"Let's go, ignore him," Old Han said; I also timidly followed him away. This was naturally disrespectful to the old priest, but the word "stealing" entered Old Han's ears, and he was not convinced; he had that kind of brute strength.

The strange thing was that the school authorities did not do anything to us the next day, even though we were disrespectful to the old priest and even insulted him by ignoring his lecture.

But Old Han was still not convinced. He met the foreign dog servant on the playground, and he beat the servant, beating him severely; saying that it was nothing to do with the school if we ate grapes.

The school recorded his demerit, the charge was bullying a worker. I remember it that way.

Let him record the demerit, we continued to steal grapes, we ran to a corner of the orchard, a place where people rarely went, and stole; until all the servants in the school carried large buckets and picked them in large quantities, and sent them to the kitchen in large quantities, we stopped stealing.

This happened three years ago, and I still remember it clearly. Looking at the grapes in the soft green light, I miss that simple Old Han very much; but I am not even clear about Old Han's life or death. I remember he was very angry when he left the school, that was the first year after the loss of the Northeast, he had no family support and could not study; he could not even find his home, he had not received a single word from home for a year; and became a person without a home. Because he owed too much money, the kitchen stopped his meals, and he left. He said, "If this place doesn't keep me, there's always a place that will." I asked him where he was going, he said he was going to take some railway trainee exam, but he didn't bring a book, I knew.

I watched the rickshaw pull him and a bundle of bedding down the hillside, all alone.

The grapes in the corner of the desk turned into rickshaw wheels turning in my head.

Copying Targets

— Le Jian

Because of staying overnight on the journey, the feeling of homesickness will hang more easily in the heart; accidentally thinking of leaving the market, this place with a bit of mystery, it has already been fourteen years that two hands can't count. Are Father's country fellows and relatives, who have not had news, still living in the market of that prehistoric era?

Fifteen and a half li, today's journey.

In the dim dawn of the morning, the simple shop by the forest, the curling morning smoke on the thatched roof, blended with the comfortable and refreshing autumn wind, weaving a dazzling scenery. In the cold room illuminated by the shell window, my slight sleep was awakened by the long cry of the pheasant and the lowing of the calf. Thinking of the first time I came to stay last night, there was no pheasant, no calf, only then did I feel that these two sounds were so fresh, the morning in the mountains was so fresh.

The shopkeeper is an elderly man, tall and burly, with a "scarecrow" type of face. He is wearing black breeches and a tough, thick homespun belt. It is said that he used to be a镖客 (Biao Ke - armed escort); although he is doing this business now, perhaps he has not forgotten the wandering life of his early years. His demeanor looks like a legendary hero; but talking to him, you only feel that he is approachable, his eyes radiating a chivalrous spirit.

"Master, getting up early!" Seeing him old in the morning, I mechanically made a bow.

"Oh! Getting up early, getting up early." He also similarly selected a bow.

"I say, on the road to the market, there can't be..."

"That, that's not very...but it just comes and goes!"

Again with a feeling of trepidation, ending this conversation: I had long known that this fifteen-and-a-half-mile mountain path was more precipitous; I was unwilling to make a detour again, lengthening this distant journey. My heart of returning is like a flowing arrow, which is unstoppable by trepidation and hesitation. Finally, I packed up my luggage again and hastily set off.

What I saw at first was still the vast plain, with sparse crape myrtles standing tall everywhere, the morning sun climbing on the yellow loess, shining into golden mountain sunshine, and crimson mountain shade. After passing a few scattered tile kilns, and passing through a few tile drying yards, the road gradually led up the mountainside, making detours on the bare mountain, and circling around the mountain slope.

A forest of long-leafed crape myrtles blocked the way ahead, and my heart began to jump nervously. They were just for the sake of making a living, or unwilling to abandon their old nest and go elsewhere, mechanically inheriting the business of their ancestors, attempting to prolong this life. They just hid in this closed, cold mountain and abducted. I am not a merchant escorting goods, I am a wanderer returning with a light body, I have traveled all over the world with a light bag, a young man like me, is he afraid of the unexpected of being kidnapped! I thought.

In the forest, I faintly heard two or three whistles, mixed with obscene, monotonous mountain songs. In an instant, unexpectedly, two men blocked the way, all in ancient clothing, clothing that could only be found in rural opera troupes.

"Hey, going to the market? Untie it, untie it!" They rushed up fiercely.

"There are guns, hey, firearms!" Another snatched my luggage.

They skillfully spread out my luggage, pulled up the clothes and shook them in the air, there was nothing; they searched my body, there was nothing either, they looked at each other frustratedly, kicked the clothes on the ground with one foot, and left contemptuously.

"Poor kid, can't figure it out but has the air of a scholar!" I packed up my luggage and walked out of the forest very borrowedly, the long leaves of the crape myrtle brushed the remaining sound of this building.

The drawn-out sigh and obscene errors rang out again through the mountain village.

Hesitation

— Cun Yin

A song like goose down, brought by the tranquil autumn wind from a small school across the street, seemed to make me even more melancholy.

That song, emitted from the sharp vocal cords of those young students, contained a pure and lively tone. However, my narrow heart was jealous and hateful of those songs. In fact, my jealousy and hatred were practical, and useless!

So, I faced the window: drinking in the autumn wind, drinking in melancholy.

When I was young, I did not receive a good education. Following my busy father, running around east and west, it has been endless for so many years. The pomegranate tree planted in front of the courtyard when I was young has grown taller than me. My grandmother's beloved cat, and herself, have also become old and frail with the passage of time. Just take that yellowish-brown cat, its right eye is already blind, and when it walks, it looks like a ghost, the deathly pallor suppressing its actions and breathing...

Ah, everything is aging, even my red wooden washbasin, which I have had since I was a child, is leaking because of old age.

In the dim light, by the morning stream, when eating lunch, I always saw my father yawning so tiredly. Yes, he is also old.

Looking at his yawns, I am deeply afraid:

"When I reach his age, maybe I will spend the whole day lying around..."

As the boring thought flashed through my mind, I returned to my childhood: "I must be a good person!" I often consoled myself like this, and my father often nagged me in a similar way.

So, on my diary, textbooks, or notebooks, I wrote: "Strive to be a good person." And I told my father:

"I want to be an accomplished young man!"

At that time, I firmly believed that my words could be fully realized. I was blindly confused by my own words. I never thought about it: "How can I be an accomplished young man?"

Time has eroded my youth. I am already hesitating on the road to middle age. I am still me! However, my father seems to be old, his nagging is also over, and when I am with him, besides a heavy sigh, I can hardly hear anything. In his heavy sigh, I woke up. I frankly admitted that my thoughts were wrong!

"I can't be as ignorant as my grandmother's cat!" I woke up. However, the heavy iron chains of middle age have already locked me.

"I can't let the heaviness of the iron chains of middle age betray my awakening!" Thinking like that, I seemed to have gained a new environment. But, I don't know how to apply my awakening?

Every day when I hear the lively songs from the school across the street, I become more and more bitter, more and more melancholy.

In just a moment, the singers will catch up with me.

When I bury my heavy head in my hands, my father sighs again. And that clear song seems to be more resonant, more brisk!

Hosting a Banquet (Continued)

— Yan

Therefore, the rumors about Master Zhu are too numerous to recount: some say he is a smuggler of salt, some say that the Shanghai drug manufacturing organization is located in Master Zhu's mansion, and even more say that Master Zhu colluded with kidnapping bosses on the sea, providing them with a place to hide the kidnapped victims... In fact, Master Zhu has never done anything criminal except try his best to make money. Taking office as an official, earning him one hundred thousand or eighty thousand, this is investing to make a profit, not a crime; he has land, which he leases to tenants to farm, and collects rent at the end of the year. Collecting rent only earns six percent interest, so Master Zhu's measuring bucket is larger than those in the rice shops, which of course cannot be said to be illegal. However, Master Zhu values ​​money too much, for example, when tenants pay rent, there is usually a lunch, eaten from the granary, but Master Zhu only deducts twenty large coins, and pastes a red note in the accounting room: "This house has many tenants, and no food is provided, each person deducts twenty large coins." This is the point where Master Zhu made enemies of people. However, those tenants can only spread rumors, they dare not fail to pay the rent, or be short a single coin; as for any disrespectful incidents towards Master Zhu, that is guaranteed not to happen, because those who come and go from Master Zhu's door are all the top figures in this town.

But Master Zhu is hosting a grand banquet today, the two black doors are wide open, rows of "Silence and Avoidance" signs are lined up on both sides, and a large door lamp hangs in the center, so that people outside the door can see everything clearly. The halls are all decorated with silver, and the sunlight shines so dazzlingly that it confuses people's eyes, and confuses people's hearts. Those top figures, of course, arrived at the Zhu mansion early in sedan chairs, which is not surprising. What is strange; according to the errand boy who sent out the invitations: this matter is very strange, Master Zhu even invited those big tenants, it looks like there will be ten or so tables of good wine and food! This is naturally a strange thing, among those who received the invitations, there was even a barefoot person (Note 3) who did not know a single character, the day before, there was some commotion in the town, everyone ran around telling each other, and everyone was suspicious of Master Zhu's sudden grand banquet, wondering if something unfortunate was about to befall everyone. Everyone gathered in the Fuxing Teahouse, and talked for a whole day, but still could not come to a conclusion. The timid ones advocated not going, but if something bad were to happen, they would not be able to escape Master Zhu's grasp anyway. Then, some people advocated going to disturb him with a big meal of meat and fish, because the country people can't eat such good wine and dishes all year round!

Thus: barefoot, wearing torn gowns, filled Master Zhu's flower hall, and the secret inside the two black doors was finally seen by them a little. Everything was fresh, unseen before, and even the big fish and meat tasted better than what they cooked at home. Everyone ate and drank until the wine had passed half a round, and the local bailiff stood up to speak. Usually, he and a group of barefoot people could only sit in the back accounting room, but now he put on a robe and gown, and said with a decent smile:

"Today Master Zhu is inviting you to drink wine, this is really... a very good thing, because, now the province is going to levy land surtax, in the town... gentlemen, because, Master Zhu is fair in his dealings, he has already... Master Zhu has reported it, Master Zhu has become the land surtax official, for you, it is also a good thing, so, please drink wine, everyone should help Master Zhu, if the county, summons you to ask questions, you have to say that Master Zhu is good... Master Zhu is good... well, everyone drink another cup of wine, understand? Master Zhu is good..." The bailiff stammered and only said half of what he had planned for a long time, he looked at Master Zhu, wondering if he had said anything wrong?

Master Zhu nodded. Master Zhu is good, those barefoot people also know, this land surtax official is another good side income. But this banquet was making trouble in everyone's stomach, and no one nodded.

Understand? Everyone understands very clearly.

(Note 1) Granary means landlord.

(Note 2) Ten halls and nine courtyards, describes the width of the house, not that there are ten houses and nine courtyards.

(Note 3) Barefoot people, means looking down on farmers.

Moving

— Simon

With each move, my mood changes, and I always sigh because of it, why do I always bother myself with some insignificant things. In the past three years, I can't remember how many times I've moved. I've lived in lively places and quiet places, and then from quiet places to lively places. When I live in a quiet area, if I don't go out all day, it's like I've forgotten the world. All I can hear is the faint sound of fruit trees swaying in the breeze outside the window. I feel too lonely, and I feel as if I've been abandoned by everyone, so I move away. When I move, of course, I move to a very lively environment. The street may be right under the window, and from early in the morning every day, the noise of various vehicles continues until late at night, and my ears are always buzzing. I simply can't do anything, and my mood can't be calmed down no matter what. I gradually become irritable, and I feel that if I delay any longer, I might become neurasthenic, so I move again. This time I move from a lively place to a quiet place. The new house is far from the city streets, and the noise of cars can only be faintly heard late at night, and it is already very scattered. This is completely suitable for me to need a longer period of quiet mood to brew. And behind the house is the neighbor's garden. Autumn is already deep, and there are no flowers to be seen. On the lawn, only tall sycamores stand proudly, and although many of the leaves are yellow, they have fallen all over the ground, showing some haggardness; but on sunny days, it can still cast a shadow on the ground. I hear a rustling sound, and then it falls down with a swish. I know that the sycamore leaves have been ravaged by a merciless wind god.

For several months, I have been exhausted and eager to find a place to rest greatly. Now the house is very suitable. If there are no accidents or anything necessary, I plan to live here for a longer period of time and not move easily anymore. In fact, my moving is very simple. There are no cumbersome things like suitcases, or even a few quilts. I can move immediately if I want to. It's just moving a person to another place. What's annoying is looking for a house. I often run around all day, and my legs are numb, but I still can't find a place that satisfies me. Once the house is found, things are over. Thinking back to the first move in the past three years, there were always cars and cars of luggage. At that time, the hardship of moving was really something. After that, every time I moved, there were fewer items, and gradually it was reduced to just a bachelor's body. Earlier, because I was worried about too many things, I was really unwilling to move, and it was also not easy to move. When I had nothing outside my body, and it was just me alone, the house could be moved. From the matter of moving, I often can't help but reminisce about the traces of my personal life during these days, and the changes. I feel a little lost; during these days I have lived in cramped pigeon cage-like attics, lived in foreign houses with beautiful interiors, lived in dark places where I couldn't even see the sunlight during the day, and also lived in places where there were elevators to replace my steps. I have seen many different neighbors, and seen the lives of many different neighbors. And myself, in the midst of moving back and forth, my feelings have gradually faded, and my thoughts have gradually become gloomy. The movement of the house is like a person's experience, sometimes facing the sun, but sometimes only seeing dark shadows. After a few more changes, I'm afraid people will be old!

Since the 6th National Games opened on Double Ten Day at the newly built sports field in the central district of this city, the eyes of the whole country have been focused on every athlete, and everyone hopes that they can establish good results and make contributions to China's sports world. Because it is small and exquisite and very beautiful, the recipients all regard it as a precious treasure. Now the company is worried that it may not be able to distribute it universally, so if anyone has not received this booklet, they can attach half a cent of postage and send it to the company's propaganda department on Nao Tal Road, and they will send a booklet immediately.

Shen Bao Special Issue of Chinese Engineering Society on Domestic Building Materials

A Brief History of Shanghai Zhenhua Paint Co., Ltd.

Zhenhua Paint Co., Ltd. was founded in the seventh year of the Republic of China (1918). The founder was the former manager, Mr. Shao Jinqing. Mr. Shao believed that paint was a necessity for building materials, with huge amounts of money flowing out of the country annually. Therefore, he collaborated with Mr. Yue Zhenbao, Mr. Wang Yunfu, and others to establish a manufacturing plant to reclaim these profits. After more than ten years of struggle and painstaking management, it finally became a leader in China's paint industry, adding a unique brilliance to the national product manufacturing industry.

The company is a joint-stock company with a capital of 200,000 national currency units. It has nine directors and supervisors, who form a board of directors. Under the board, there is a general manager and an assistant manager, each executing all affairs. The current general manager is Mr. Qin Jingcheng, and the assistant manager is Mr. Song Peidao. The manufacturing plant is located at Tanzi Bay, Zhongshan Road, Zhabei, Shanghai, covering an area of over ten acres. It faces the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway in the front and relies on the Suzhou River in the back, making both land and water transportation extremely convenient. The factory buildings are constructed with the latest style of cement and steel frames. Inside, they are divided into sections for thick paint, blending, oil refining, varnish, water powder, lead powder, and red lead. All machinery is powered by electricity, employing over a hundred workers. A branch factory is set up in Tianjin and is currently undergoing expansion. There are a total of four distribution offices. The main distribution office is located at 478-480 North Suzhou Road, Shanghai. Branch distribution offices are located at Baocheng Road in Hankou, Jiankang Road in Nanjing, and Xinmin Road in Hangzhou. There are over fifty managers and distributors in various ports. The sales destinations include not only China but also the Nanyang Islands, British and Dutch territories, and places like Roro (likely a misspelling). Overseas Chinese compatriots are mostly happy to purchase the products.

The products include:

(1) Thick paint, (2) Blending paint, (3) Anti-rust paint, (4) House paint, (5) Sanding paint, (6) Automotive enamel, (7) Quick-drying enamel, (8) Varnish, (9) Wood paint, (10) Refined paint, (11) Pore filler, (12) Water powder, (13) Red lead, (14) Lead powder, (15) Paint oil, etc., totaling more than ten types. The trademarks are Flying Tiger, Double Flag, Three Sheep, Tai Chi, Invincible, and Peony, totaling six types. The annual production volume reaches over 2,600 tons. The most famous products are superior white paint, boiled oil, improved gold paint, quick-drying enamel, and the recently released water powder paint. Except for a portion of pigments ordered from European and American countries, the remaining raw materials are all domestic products.

In addition to the paint manufacturing section, the factory also has a chemical testing department that specializes in analyzing the composition of various raw materials and products and researching methods for improvement. Furthermore, the engineering department specializes in designing and undertaking various paint projects for all sectors. Recently, they have compiled a kind of artistic pattern, which makes painted houses elegant and beautiful, and is also a unique feature.

The former Ministry of Industry and Commerce of the National Government, due to the company's excellent products, once requested the Ministry of Navy, Army and Air Force, as well as the provincial and municipal governments, to instruct their subordinates to adopt them as much as possible. Currently, the Jinghu, Huhangyong, Beining, Jinpu, Jiaoji, Pingsui, Longhai, Daoqing, and Nanxun railways, as well as the construction bureaus and public works bureaus of various provinces and cities, post offices, and China Merchants Group, all adopt them. Even foreign-operated companies such as the Shanghai British Tramway Company and Taikoo Dockyard frequently use them to paint vehicles and ships, adding a lot of glory to national products.

The establishment of the company is entirely based on the principle of promoting national products. It is never complacent about various products and strives for excellence. In the future, it should particularly work hard on research to ensure that all products become even better.

Talking About Fire Bricks

Fire bricks are extremely important in the industrial sector, especially in heavy industry and kiln-fired industries like enamel and glass. Ceramic products have a very long history in our country. In theory, the manufacturing and application of related refractory materials should have significant advantages. However, the reality shows us that China's industrial sector is always stuck in old ways and is not easy to improve. Even considering the kilns in Yixing, the most famous place for kiln products in our country, and the kiln houses in Jiangxi porcelain manufacturing factories, they are still built with locally made earthen bricks and tiles. In recent years, the mechanical industry has become increasingly developed. Almost every factory has a boiler as a necessity. The materials for building furnaces are definitely not something that old earthen bricks and tiles can handle. The importance of fire bricks is increasing daily. Until recently, the source of fire bricks completely depended on foreign countries. Since the establishment of the Kailuan Coal Mines, due to its own needs, it set up a fire brick manufacturing factory in Tangshan (where there are excellent raw materials nearby). Later, due to the pressing needs of the outside world, things fell into place, and it became their side business. Everyone knows that Kailuan is a foreign-owned mining company. Seeing that money was still flowing out, the Chinese recently started to manufacture domestic fire bricks.

The main raw materials for fire bricks are a mixture of natural refractory stone and kaolin clay. Our country has excellent raw materials everywhere, so there is no need to rely on foreign countries. The most important condition for fire bricks is that they must have particularly strong refractoriness and pressure resistance. The durability of each boiler and kiln, and the quality of its products, all depend on how these two strengths determine its fate. Due to the importance of the relationship, the industrial sector is extremely strict in procurement. Due to the lack of precision in technology and raw materials, the quality of domestic fire bricks varies greatly, which is often criticized by industrialists who promote national products, and there is still a tendency to trust foreign goods.

Mr. Hu Zu'an of Dinghai founded the China Kiln Industry Company in the 21st year of the Republic (1932). Through four years of hard work, the Earth Brand fire bricks produced have, in addition to the two main conditions of high refractoriness and high pressure resistance, paid more attention to reducing shrinkage and ensuring the accuracy of custom shapes. It has established a very good reputation in the domestic industrial sector. A simple introduction is given here to seek common promotion and reverse the fate of domestic fire bricks.

Domestic Tar Felt

— Loss

Tar felt is an essential material for preventing leaks on roofs, occupying an important position in the construction industry. In the past, our country did not produce it, so all requirements were met by imports. The annual loss is more than millions of dollars. Now, engineer Mr. Cao Kedong has been researching and carefully manufacturing in Tianjin for many years. He has now raised funds to establish the Jianhua Industrial Company in Tianjin, specializing in the production of various oil felts to meet the needs of various constructions in our country. The price is low and the quality is good, enough to seize the position of foreign goods and replace them. In various ports in North China, the sales are extremely wide, and all owners praise each other. Now, in response to the needs of major construction projects in Shanghai, a resident office has been specially established at No. 41, Lane 2, East De'an Lane, North Shanxi Road, and major hardware stores in this port are entrusted with sales, so that those who purchase for various construction projects can easily procure them. It is hoped that major architects and construction factories will enthusiastically promote them to increase the glory of national products and plug the leaks. This is what we deeply hope for.

After Visiting the Gymnasium and Swimming Pool Built by the Municipal Government

The Shanghai Municipal Government, for the sake of promoting sports, built a gymnasium and swimming pool in the twenty-third year of the Republic of China (1934) to provide the citizens of this city with opportunities to exercise their bodies in their spare time and to have legitimate entertainment venues for sports competitions. The Sixth National Games was held in Shanghai this time, and it was a great opportunity to use this building. On the day of the completion of the above two buildings, the reporter visited the interior. Most of the construction materials used were domestic products. For example, the steel windows were contracted by the China Copper and Iron Factory. It is said that all the steel windows of the Nanjing Ministry of Transportation Building were also manufactured by this factory. They are fine, strong and very durable. The mosaics in the swimming pool are produced by Xingye Tile Company.

(1) Gymnasium, located north of the swimming pool, facing east. The house style adopts a mixed style of modern and Chinese architecture. All exterior walls are made of red bricks and have artificial stone carvings, so the appearance is very majestic, and the interior is exquisite and magnificent. It was designed by architect Dong Dayou of the Municipal Central District Construction Committee and built by Chengtai Construction Factory. The main entrance of the hall has a lobby ticket office, a hall, men's and women's toilets, aisles, passageways, basketball courts, gyms, offices, meeting rooms, dressing rooms, bathrooms, sports equipment rooms, kitchens, and boiler rooms. The boiler rooms were contracted by Guangyonghe Boiler Factory. The arrangement is orderly. The grandstand has a capacity of 2,500 seated and 1,500 standing.

(2) Swimming Pool, built according to the dimensions of American university swimming and competition regulations. The outdoor style has grandstands built on all four sides, with a capacity of 5,000 seated and 1,000 standing. The length of the pool is eighty feet, the width is twenty feet, the depth of the pool is two feet at the shallowest end, and twenty-one (the rest is missing), the capacity (missing). The bottom and sides of the pool are paved with mosaics, clean and often. The water filtration and lighting equipment in the pool are particularly characteristic. Next to this pool, a small swimming pool is built for children to swim.

Inside the pool, from the main entrance, there is a hall ticket office, a furnace room, men's and women's toilets, vertical and horizontal aisles, a living room, an office, a cloakroom, a lounge, a swimming equipment room, a dressing room, a sales office, etc. The layout is thoughtful, tidy and elegant, and it is the best-equipped swimming pool in China.

History of Steel Window Factories in Our Country

Our country's steel window factories started in the fourteenth year of the Republic of China (1925). The earliest founder was China Copper and Iron Factory. In addition to specializing in the manufacture of steel windows and steel doors, the factory also contracted various copper and iron projects. The general manager, Mr. Li Xianyao, once served as the Chinese manager of a British steel window factory for more than ten years, so he has in-depth research on the construction principles of steel windows. Afterwards, he set up his own factory at No. 513, Haifang Road, covering an area of four acres. Recently, due to the development of business, a second factory was added at Song Park Road, Liuying Road. The equipment in the factory is all new-style machinery, and all management adopts scientific management methods. Therefore, the products are excellent and fast. Usually, the number of employed workers is about 160 to 170. For example, the National Government Ministry of Transportation Building, the National Government Civil Service Office Building, the Supreme Court Building, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs official residence building, the official residence of Chairman Chiang, the Executive Yuan office building, the offices of various bureaus of the Shanghai Municipal Government, the Municipal Central Transportation Bureau, the Huaye Building, the residence of Mr. Wang Boqun, the residence of Mr. Wang Jingwei, the residence of Mr. Kong Xiangxi, the residence of Mr. Chen Gongbo, the residence of Mr. Zeng Zhongming, the residence of Mr. Hu Yunqiu, the residence of Mr. Ye Chu, the Central Health Administration, the Central Epidemic Prevention Office, the Central Medical Administration College, the Shanghai Tuberculosis Sanatorium, the China Leprosy Sanatorium, the Shanghai Municipal Hygiene Laboratory, the Central Bank Warehouse, the Hongkou Bank of China, the Hongkou Four Lines Savings Society, the Bank of Communications Warehouse, the Bank of China Warehouse, the Qingdao Jin Cheng Bank, the Qingdao Dalu Bank, the Jinan Dalu Bank, the Tianchu MSG Factory, the Tianli Light Gas Factory, the Shanghai Municipal Gymnasium, the Shanghai Municipal Swimming Pool, the News Newspaper Office, and the steel windows used in this museum were all contracted and installed by (missing), and they have been there for many years (missing) bad, enough (missing) the excellence of the factory's products.
