The company's first and second factories have a total of seven new-style (missing), which can produce more than 700 square feet of mosaic porcelain and more than 400 square feet of glazed wall tiles per month. The Four Lines Savings Society Building, which has already been completed, and the Wing On Company's seventeen-story new building, which is under construction, are the first to adopt them. Other giant buildings under construction, such as the Great Sun Company on Nanjing Road, are also scrambling to the company, looking at samples and ordering goods. Generally, construction operators are all considered to be the latest and most beautiful building materials in 1935. The company's first factory is located in Yangjing, Pudong, and the second factory is located on Huo Bilan Road. The general office is located at No. 89 Fuzhou Road. All products have samples, and all sectors are welcomed to visit and purchase. The reception is said to be diligent.

An Overview of the Huaxin Brick and Tile Company

Huaxin Brick and Tile Company was founded in the eleventh year of the Republic of China (1922). At that time, the scale was not complete, and there was only one type of large flat tile. Later, Mr. Liu Zixian, the manager of the company, left Taishan Brick and Tile Company and came to preside over the company, which made major reforms. In the past five or six years, the scale has been complete, and there have been various types of flat tiles, Spanish tiles, barrel tiles, and Chinese temple-style barrel tiles. Mr. Liu has long served as the chief engineer of Taishan Company. He has excellent technology and rich experience. All products made by him are exquisite and unique, and are praised by the construction industry.

In the spring of the twenty-second year of the Republic of China (1933), Mr. Liu saw that the cement flower tiles on the cars were mostly bad and could not be used for a long time, so he studied them carefully and gained a lot of experience. Therefore, he expanded the scope, purchased the latest type of (missing) press with 2,500 pounds per square inch, and used high-quality flint and pigments to make beautiful flower tiles, which are no different from foreign goods.

Huaxin flower tiles have accurate dimensions, solid texture, clear patterns, and a smooth tile surface, which are unmatched by other flower tiles. Since its sales, it has spread all over the ports. The most notable are the Nanjing National Government Auditorium, Chairman Lin's villa, the Central Party Department Party History, the Capital Hotel, the Jiangsu Bank, the Agricultural College of Zhejiang University in Hangzhou, the Aviation School Sports Ground, the Dongwu University Affiliated Middle School in Huzhou, the Nanchang Provincial Government Office Building, and the Aviation School, the Jiujiang Central Bank, the Shanghai French Concession Public Works Bureau, the Lagrange Chinese Public School, the residences of senior officers of the Bank of China, Mr. Du Yuesheng's villa, and the Da Sun Company, which is under construction, all use the company's flower tiles for paving. The popularity of the company's products can be seen from this.

Domestic Asbestos Products in Shanghai

In recent years, China's industrial construction and machinery have become increasingly developed, and the demand for asbestos products has been increasing day by day. Because demand exceeds supply, the loss of imports each year is no less than millions of dollars. In the beginning, I didn't know that there were asbestos manufacturers in China. Recently, due to the high price of foreign goods and the slow delivery, I had to investigate in China to see if there were asbestos manufacturers in China. After... three weeks, the first one found was "Zhen'an Asbestos Factory", and the second one was "Dadong Asbestos Factory". Before discovering each factory, I always thought that the asbestos products bought from hardware stores were foreign goods. After investigation, it was not the case. More than half of what hardware stores sell are bought in China, because Chinese goods are not inferior to foreign goods, and the effectiveness is the same. In particular, the price is half cheaper than foreign goods! Sometimes foreign goods managers, for fear of being fined for delayed delivery, the first remedy is to order goods from Chinese factories and change the signs to deceive the users. This proves that Chinese goods are applicable, and further proves that people who blindly believe in foreign goods are blindly following. Now I will write down a few points below for the reference of the construction industry:

Raw Materials Asbestos is a kind of stony ore, the color has red, white, green, black, yellow, etc., the length is different, the longest is more than two feet, the shortest is less than an inch, the color is the best with white and soft. The stone blocks are mined from the mine, and after a series of refining and grinding procedures by the manufacturer, the result is a fibrous material selected from a hard stone layer; this kind of material is asbestos, its characteristics are non-combustible, winter is warm, summer is cold, and it is insulated and hemostatic. It is very easy to test the authenticity of asbestos. Just burn it with fire and you will immediately get a definite answer.

Mining Area In addition to a small part of Sichuan Province, the asbestos mining area in Hebei Province (missing) the widest, and the output is the most abundant in Laiyuan. The Sichuan Province mining area is difficult to exploit and the transportation is inconvenient, so it has not been exploited, because after exploitation, the value of transportation to the mainland is too far from the Laiyuan goods. The supply of asbestos raw materials in the country now completely relies on Laiyuan's output. The company that holds the mining rights of the Laiyuan mining area is Tianjin Zhenye Asbestos Factory.

Factories In Shanghai, the largest commercial port in China; there are many factories and water and land terminals; it is impossible to find a complete asbestos product factory, and Dadong is more complete than the general vendors selling asbestos mud, but Dadong is only limited to asbestos pipes and asbestos bricks. Other goods are still lacking. Recently, the products of Zhenye Asbestos Factory, which was established by Tianjin, are indeed complete, because its factory has mines and the machinery is more complete, so there are many kinds of products, but its manufacturing department is in Tianjin, and Zhenye's goods are cheaper.

Types There are many types of asbestos products. To divide them in detail, there are more than a hundred types. The current Chinese products include the following: asbestos raw rope, asbestos square rope, asbestos lead wire raw rope, asbestos lead wire square rope, asbestos various rubber core packing, asbestos various lead powder packing, asbestos loose rope, the above goods are all from 3/8 inch diameter to 3 inches, asbestos wire is from 2.5 mm to 3/8 inch, asbestos paper board is from 2.5 mm thick to 4/8 inch, asbestos brick, asbestos pipe, asbestos tile, asbestos belt, asbestos mud, asbestos gloves, asbestos shoe covers, asbestos cloth, asbestos clothes, asbestos pants, asbestos vest, asbestos hair cap, asbestos various washers, asbestos pillow, asbestos fiber, asbestos furnace opening, asbestos lamp wick, etc., each item is measured by foot or by pound, each item's humidity, tensile strength, and fire power are the same as foreign goods.

Uses Asbestos has great uses. In addition to the large sales market for building materials, asbestos is also an indispensable thing for machinery, boilers, trains, warships, shipyards, airplanes, ordnance factories, mints, yarn factories, vaults, fire brigades, various factories, and even safes.

The above sections are just written casually based on what I know, but I dare not talk nonsense about the details of the asbestos root, I hope that the gentlemen in the domestic asbestos industry will express their opinions more, to increase the knowledge of all sectors of society about asbestos, and it is also enough to promote and sell it.

An Overview of Shanghai Tai Kee Asbestos Factory

Founding Overview The factory was founded in the fifteenth year of the Republic of China (1926). In the beginning, the factory used asbestos coating, (namely, commonly known as paper and cypress mud) and relied on foreign countries a lot, and the annual loss was extremely considerable. Because its manufacture is simple, it initiated the establishment of a factory to manufacture it by itself. Then, it gradually invented asbestos magnesium rust powder, magnesium rust block, and magnesium rust pipe, etc. In addition to supplying most of the factories, it also occupies an important position for the needs of the construction industry and sanitation engineering with the trend of the times and the improvement of science. It is indeed a sharp weapon to resist foreign goods and a glorious page of national products. The factory has expanded year by year, and the management occupies several acres of land, and has become a giant in the asbestos industry.

Domestic Stone The raw materials of the factory are mostly from Sichuan and the north, and the attached supplies are also from Jiangsu and Zhejiang, which can be called completely domestic goods. It is definitely not the same as other kinds of crafts, which are remanufactured with foreign raw materials and called domestic goods.

Excellent Manufacturing The factory's manufacturing motivation is electric machinery, such as rolling bullets, mixing, pressing tops, baking spray, bleaching, and models, all designed and manufactured by themselves, so most of the products are made by machinery, which are uniform and tidy, and there is no drawback of unevenness.

Product Features First, let's talk about the most common asbestos coating. Generally, the white ones manufactured on the market are mostly mixed with a small amount of raw materials. This kind is not only unusable, but also requires more than ten pounds per square foot according to the usage calculation, while the factory only needs seven pounds. If the same price, the actual use of the factory is cost-effective and reliable. This section must be paid attention to by users. Secondly, it must have "firmness" and "resistance". The factory's raw materials are of high quality, the tendons are long and the strength is sufficient, and each package contains rich raw materials and good adhesion. Therefore, once it is coated on boilers or water pipes, it is unusually "firm", and there is absolutely no drawback of difficult work and patterns. All engineering that involves coating boilers, water pipes, and fireproof insulation requires "sufficient resistance". The hot steam in boilers and water pipes will not leak out, which can save fuel, and the vaults and silver boxes will not be invaded by fire, which can ensure eternal peace. As for magnesium rust powder, magnesium rust block, magnesium rust pipe, and other raw materials, because the value is higher than asbestos and coatings, the effect is even greater. Looking back at the many large projects of the factory, the results are all satisfactory, which is ironclad proof. I dare to introduce it as above.

A Brief History of Taishan Brick and Tile Company

Taishan Brick and Tile Company was founded in the tenth year of the Republic of China (1921) by founders Huang Shoumin, Qian Xinzhi, Nie Yuntai, Hu Xuanming and others with a capital of 50,000 yuan to open a factory in Jiashan, Zhejiang to manufacture ordinary blue and red bricks and tiles. Due to good management, the products were quite popular in society. Soon, with the rise of architecture in Shanghai, new-style bricks and tiles all came from foreign countries. It was planned to imitate them and compete with them. Therefore, on the one hand, people were sent to the United States to investigate and practice to further their studies. On the other hand, the share capital was expanded to one million yuan, with a paid-up capital of 250,000 yuan. The second factory was selected to be built in Xinlonghua, Shanghai, purchasing a total of 200 acres of land, building twelve American-style kiln piers, and various manufacturing machines were also purchased from the United States. The original engine was purchased from Germany. New-style equipment such as heating rooms using hot air and electric meters controlling kiln temperature were all available. At that time, the products of both factories were better than those of other companies, and they successively won the highest-class medals from the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, the Commodity Exhibition, and the Jiangsu Provincial Commodity Exhibition. In the spring of the fifteenth year of the Republic of China (1926), the company's unique thin-style bricks were born, which were magnificent, beautiful, strong, and durable. People from all walks of life praised them. The great buildings in Shanghai and the capital, such as the twenty-two-story Four Lines Savings Society, the Broadway Building, the eighteen-story Junling Building, and the new buildings of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Railways in Nanjing, and the Central Hospital and the Department of Health, almost all used Taishan facing bricks. A section chief of the Shanghai Municipal Public Works Bureau wrote that the most innovative domestic materials in the past twenty years should be the thin-style facing bricks, which is indeed a correct statement. The National Government and the Shanghai Municipal Government both rewarded the creation, so they specially gave Taishan Company a ten-year patent for manufacturing thin-style facing bricks. Taishan Company's red tiles and blue tiles are also the best of their kind, so it is not without reason that the market calls the best tiles Taishan tiles. Recently, in order to expand, the company has specially hired porcelain experts who graduated from the United States as technicians to research and improve products, and added two giant kiln piers to specialize in firing glazed bricks and tiles, art tiles, and new products such as Taishan stones, which proves that the company's general manager, Mr. Huang Shoumin, is dedicated to his work and strives for excellence. The future development is unlimited.

"Locks" are indispensable building materials. A metal factory specializes in manufacturing all kinds of tumbler locks, such as wooden door locks, steel door locks (missing) door locks, cabinet door locks, drawer locks, steel tool locks, safe locks, steel window locks, and other more than 30 kinds of good quality and low price. They are not inferior to foreign goods and are displayed on the table of the association.
